Framer-motion usage is only 4 files, and `router.tsx` shows three suspects before profiling: `AnimatePresence mode="wait"` serializes exit → (possible blank `Suspense fallback={null}` gap on lazy chunks) → enter, so every nav starts with a built-in 200ms+ delay; the transition animates `opacity`+`y` on a div wrapping the whole textured `Page` (data-URI SVG `feTurbulence` parchment), forcing per-frame repaints of an expensive surface; and `key={pathname}` remounts the full page tree so mount-time loads contend with the entrance animation. 4 phases: profile-first (confirm/kill suspects against the live dev server), fix the route transition (opacity-only crossfade, no mode="wait", no blank gap — or remove it entirely per the motion-restraint principle if that's what smooth takes), simplify what stays (shared transition config, CSS where framer is overkill, keep the Stack slide), gate with checks + real-page smoothness verification in Chrome. - [[IDEA-67]] (new, all 4 phases): replaced the dirty-sync agent with deterministic git, and made the `stale-merged` gate actually fire after a GitHub-side merge. Motivation got a live proof mid-session: the user clicked IDEA-66's sync button, the sync agent stashed their uncommitted work ("sync-idea-66: uncommitted work before switching to main"), checked out main, and never popped — exactly the "model re-decides stash-or-commit per run" failure the idea predicts (work recovered from `stash@{0}` by hand). Changes: `runGitSync` (`git.ts`) now stash-carries a dirty tree (`stash push --include-untracked` → checkout/fetch/ff-merge → `stash pop`), with a pop conflict throwing a clear "originals are still in `git stash`" error that never masks a primary sync failure; `/api/git/sync` (`routes/git.ts`) lost the clean/dirty `mode` split, the `DIRTY_SYNC_PROMPT`, and the `agent.startSync` path (also removed from `agent.ts` + the `AgentManager` interface — the `sync` TaskKind stays so historical `tasks.log` rows render); `syncToMain()` (`git-api.ts`) and `handleSync` (`commit-section.tsx`) dropped the mode plumbing. Hygiene: new `mainRef()` in `git.ts` resolves `origin/main` when the ref exists (falling back to `main`), used by both `isMergedIntoMain` and the behind-count — the local `main` ref only advances on checkout+pull, so comparing against it meant a PR merged on GitHub never looked merged (live repro on PR #46) — plus a 60s-throttled fire-and-forget `git fetch origin main` kicked from `getBranchHygieneStatus` so the flip happens without a manual fetch. 3 new real-repo tests (dirty carry incl. untracked; pop conflict rejects with `papercamp-sync` stash preserved; `stale-merged` detected via `origin/main` while local `main` is stale). `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check .`, and `pnpm test` all clean (325 tests, +3).
- [[IDEA-66]] follow-up (new phase 3): on a `stale-merged` branch the sync button now REPLACES the commit controls (suggest wand, title input, message textarea, Commit button) in `commit-section.tsx`'s has-changes state instead of stacking under them — committing on a merged branch only strands more work off main, so the card offers one action, the right one, with no disabled Commit button to explain; the changed-files accordion stays visible above so what the sync will carry is still inspectable. Also diagnosed why the gate never fired in the real workflow: `getBranchHygieneStatus` compares against the LOCAL `main` ref (`git branch --merged main`, `rev-list HEAD..main`), which only advances on checkout+pull — the very thing sync does — so after a GitHub-side merge the branch never looked merged (live repro: PR #46 merged, HEAD an ancestor of origin/main, hygiene still `dirty`). Unblocked this checkout with `git fetch origin main:main` (fast-forwards the ref without touching the worktree; hygiene flipped to `stale-merged` on the next status poll). The systemic fix — compare hygiene against `origin/main` with a throttled background fetch — is deliberately NOT in this change (this tree is about to be dirty-synced); file it as its own idea next. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check .`, and `pnpm test` all clean (322 tests, unchanged); verified live in Chrome — Commit card shows only the file list + "Branch merged — sync to main".

Common state, since every agent run dirties `papercamp/tasks.log`/`.task-logs/`. Fix: `commit-section.tsx`'s has-changes branch now renders a full-width "Branch merged — sync to main" button (plus the existing `syncError` alert) under the Commit button, gated on `gitBranchHygiene === 'stale-merged'` — the server-side status that already means "merged into main AND main advanced past it, dirty or not". Reuses `handleSync` untouched; gating keeps the escape hatch out of the commit form during normal work so a mid-work sync can't be clicked by accident. Next phase (make the header labels sortable buttons) should replace the `<span style={headerLabelStyle}>` cells with real `<button>`s and set `aria-sort` directly on the grid's own container elements — there's no paper-ui seam being bypassed since the current header isn't paper-ui `Table` markup. - [[IDEA-65]] fix-review verdict semantics: after e31c7dd's parser fix, the 12:18 fix-review run settled correctly ("Resolved 1/1 review threads, replied to 3" — thread resolution and skip-replies both landed on PR #43 under the user's account, and CodeRabbit even accepted one skip-reply and resolved that thread itself). What stayed open were exactly the comments whose skip reason was "Already fixed in an earlier commit": the prompt defined `addressed` as "comments you actually fixed [in this run]", so the agent honestly filed already-fixed ones under `skipped`, which only posts a reply and never resolves. Re-worded the two contract lines in `buildFixReviewPrompt` (`prompts.ts`): `addressed` now means "the current code genuinely settles this, whether fixed in this run or by an earlier commit", and the changed-nothing rule now says already-settled comments still go in `addressed` — so a re-run resolves stale-but-fixed threads instead of stranding them open with an "already fixed" reply. No parser/settle code change needed; prompt text only. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check .`, and `pnpm test` all clean (322 tests, unchanged — the prompts test asserts the JSON keys, not the prose).
- [[IDEA-65]] fix-review settle bug: the "resolve PR threads when fixes land" flow (`settleReviewThreads` in `agent.ts` — resolve addressed threads, reply-with-reason to skipped ones) silently no-oped on both of today's fix-review runs. Root cause: `parseFixReviewResult` took `task.lines.findLast(non-empty)` and `JSON.parse`d it, but (a) the model wrapped its final verdict in a ```json fence despite the prompt's "no code fences" (prompts.ts step 5), and (b) the claude-code adapter pushes a whole multi-line text block as ONE `lines` entry, so the "last line" was the entire final message ending in a fence — unparseable, verdict `undefined`, settle skipped, only the generic "verify manually" warning in the task log (visible in `papercamp/.task-logs/6f3874d8….log`, which even shows a perfectly valid `{"addressed": [3,5,6,7], …}` verdict that never got used). The threads that did get resolved on GitHub were resolved by CodeRabbit's own post-push verification, which masked the breakage. Fix: `parseFixReviewResult` now flattens `task.lines` to physical lines (`flatMap(split('\n'))`) and scans backwards for the last line starting with `{` that passes the full verdict validation (extracted to `validateFixReviewVerdict`, same exactly-once partition rules) — fences and prose can't parse, an earlier echoed snippet can't win over the real final verdict, and a fenced-but-valid verdict now settles threads. Added a regression test reproducing the exact failure (summary prose + fenced verdict → result still parsed, no "verify manually" warning). `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check .`, and `pnpm test` all clean (322 tests, +1 new).
- [[IDEA-65]] review feedback (UI polish): reworked the two surfaces the review called out as off-style. Tasks page (`tasks-page.tsx`): dropped paper-ui's generic `Table` for the house table-shaped-list-of-Cards pattern from `plan-rows.tsx` — a kraft header card over canvas row cards sharing a new `.task-rows-grid` column template (chevron / Task / Plan / Agent / Started / Ended / Outcome; the two mono timestamp columns get a compact `dd/mm hh:mm:ss` format and collapse below 1024px via `.task-rows-cell-time`, mirroring `.plan-rows-cell-updated`). Clicking a row unfolds its persisted log as a kraft card under the row (chevron rotates via `.task-rows-chevron`, matching Table's affordance; the `<pre>` is capped at 320px with its own scroll); a Stack card's click-through still lands highlighted (`.task-row-highlighted` now rings the row + its log together) and additionally auto-expands that row. `ChevronRightIcon` is inlined in `tasks-page.tsx` since the installed paper-ui 0.7.5 doesn't export it (only Table uses it internally). Two `biome-ignore lint/a11y/useSemanticElements` suppressions on the clickable row divs — the agent card nests the Stop `IconButton` (a native `<button>` can't contain a button) and the task row wraps a `Card` whose block layout a button would break; both keep keyboard handlers. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check .`, and `pnpm test` all clean (321 tests, unchanged — pure presentation). Verified in Chrome against the live dev server: separate agent cards, consistent tasks list, working expand + highlight/scroll click-through.
- [[IDEA-65]] phase 11 (final): made a Stack Agent card's click-through navigate to its own task-page entry instead of carrying an inline log preview. `agent-section.tsx`'s `AgentTaskCard` dropped its `Accordion`/last-line log preview entirely (that detail now lives solely on the Tasks page from phases 6/10) and its outer `div` gained an `onClick` (`useNavigate` → `/tasks` with `search: { taskId: task.id }`); the Stop `IconButton`'s `onClick` calls `e.stopPropagation()` first so clicking Stop no longer also triggers the navigation. `router.tsx`'s `/tasks` route gained a `validateSearch` returning `{ taskId?: string }`. `tasks-page.tsx` reads that via `useSearch({ from: '/tasks' })`, passes `rowKey`/`rowClassName` to `Table` so the matching row gets a `task-row-highlighted` class (new rule in `utilities.css`, identical ring to the existing `.plan-row-highlighted`), and scrolls it into view on mount — same `containerRef.current?.querySelector(...)?.scrollIntoView(...)` pattern `list-view.tsx` already uses for plan rows. A running task still has nothing in its per-task log file until it finishes (phase 10 only persists lines on completion), so the highlighted row for an in-flight task shows no expandable content yet — a known gap, not addressed here since the plan's phase list didn't call for merging live status into the Tasks page. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `pnpm test` all clean (321 tests, unchanged — a click-through/routing change with no new assertable server-side surface). 11/11 phases now checked — set `status: review` in this idea's frontmatter (a human still promotes to `done`).
- [[IDEA-65]] phase 10: persisted each finished task's output lines so a past task's page has something to show after a restart, not just `tasks.log`'s `{id, kind, title, agent, start/end, outcome}` summary. `logTaskCompletion()` in `agent.ts` (the one place every terminal transition already routes through, per phase 6) now also writes `task.lines.join('\n')` to a new per-task file (`taskLogFile(root, id)` in `helpers.ts`, resolving to `papercamp/.task-logs/<id>.log` — a dotfile dir alongside the corpus, distinct from `tasks.log` itself), `mkdir`'d first since the dir doesn't exist yet on a fresh checkout; best-effort like the JSONL append next to it. Added a new `GET /api/tasks/log?id=` route (`server/routes/tasks.ts`, wired into `buildRoutes`) — a query-param `Route` rather than a `ReadRoute` since `ReadRoute` handlers get no `req` to read `?id=` off; validates `id` against a UUID regex before touching the filesystem so an arbitrary path can't be built from the query string. Client: `fetchTaskLogLines(id)` in `docs-api.ts`, and the Tasks page (`tasks-page.tsx`) now passes `expandable={{ render: (row) => <TaskLogLines id={row.id} /> }}` to its `Table` — a small component that lazily fetches a row's persisted lines only once that row is expanded, so the page never loads the whole history's output up front. Added a test proving a finished task's lines land in its per-task file matching what `getStatus()` reported live, polling the read since the write is fire-and-forget off `setStatus()` and can land slightly after the status flips to `done`. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `pnpm test` all clean (321 tests, +1 new). 10/11 phases now checked; plan frontmatter `status` stays `planned` (1 phase remains: link a Stack card to its task page).
- [[IDEA-65]] phase 9: registered `runReadOnlyPrompt`'s tasks (`commit-suggest`/`overlap-check`) in the `tasks` registry so they finally show up in `getStatus()`/the Stack — previously they logged to `tasks.log` on completion (phase 6) but were never added to `tasks`, so a running commit-suggest was invisible to the UI the whole time it ran. Added `registerTask(task)` right before `setStatus(task, 'running')` in `runReadOnlyPrompt`. Since `admit()`'s write-set gate (phase 2) now sees these tasks too, gave `writeSetFor` a `READONLY_KINDS` case returning a new `{ scope: 'none' }` variant that `writeSetsCollide` always treats as non-colliding — without it, these kinds would have fallen through to the gate's fail-closed `worktree` default and started blocking every other launch, the opposite of the fix. Also removed the now-redundant `readOnlyProcs` `Set<ChildProcess>` that `killCurrent()` swept separately for these processes' shutdown cleanup (phase 8): now that their tasks live in the `tasks` registry like everything else, `killCurrent()`'s existing `tasks.values()` sweep already reaches them, so the parallel tracking set was dead weight. Added a test proving a read-only task is visible mid-run (`status: 'running'` in `getStatus()`) and does not block a concurrent `start()` launch. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `pnpm test` all clean (320 tests, +1 new). 9/11 phases now checked; plan frontmatter `status` stays `planned` (2 phases remain: persist each task's log lines, and link a Stack card to its task page).
- [[IDEA-65]] phase 8 (final): made `killCurrent()` in `agent.ts` tear down every running child, not just the most-recently-launched task. The old implementation only ever killed `currentTask()` — the single most-recently-launched slot — so once phase 3's registry let several write-disjoint tasks run at once (or phase 1's untracked read-only prompts run alongside anything), a SIGINT/SIGTERM from the config plugin's shutdown handler (`vite.app.config.ts`) would orphan every other live child instead of reaping it. `killCurrent()` now loops `tasks.values()` and kills any task whose `proc` isn't already killed. That still missed `commit-suggest`/`overlap-check` runs from `runReadOnlyPrompt`, which are deliberately never added to the `tasks` registry (see phase 1/2's doc comments) — so those processes were invisible to both the old and the naively-fixed `killCurrent()`. Added a separate `readOnlyProcs = new Set<ChildProcess>()`, populated on spawn and pruned on the process's own `close` event, and had `killCurrent()` sweep that set too, so every child this manager can ever spawn is reachable from shutdown regardless of which registry (if any) tracks its task metadata. No behavior change to any other surface (`getStatus`/`stop`/etc. stay single-task-shaped per the plan's phase-4 note — turning those into a full multi-task surface was out of scope here). `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `pnpm test` all clean (319 tests, unchanged — shutdown-path cleanup has no assertable surface without spawning and SIGINT-ing a real subprocess). 8/8 phases now checked — set `status: review` in this idea's frontmatter (a human still promotes to `done`).
- [[IDEA-65]] phase 7: added a Tasks page that reads the persisted log from phase 6 (`papercamp/tasks.log`) and renders it as a table, surviving a dev-server restart. Server: new `parseTaskLog(raw)` in `core/parse/parser.ts` (JSON Lines — one `TaskLogEntry` per line, skipping blank/malformed lines rather than failing the whole read, since a truncated last line from a crash shouldn't hide the rest) plus a new `/api/tasks` `ReadRoute` in `reads.ts` returning `{ entries }`, same shape as `/api/progress`/`/api/suggestions`. Client: `fetchTaskLog` (`docs-api.ts`), a `taskLog`/`taskLogLoading`/`loadTaskLog` slice in `app-store.ts` mirroring `progress`'s load-with-catch-reset pattern, and a new `src/app/features/tasks/tasks-page.tsx` — a `Table` (kind/plan/agent/started/ended/outcome, outcome rendered as a green/rose `Stamp`) sorted newest-`endedAt`-first, loaded via its own mount-time `useEffect` (matching how `docs-sidebar.tsx` loads `progress`/`repoDocs` lazily rather than eagerly in the router, since this page has no sidebar to host that effect). Wired a new `/tasks` route and "Tasks" nav item into `router.tsx`, lazy-loaded like Docs/Settings; deliberately left off `hasSidebar` since the log is a flat table with nothing to filter yet. Added 3 new `parseTaskLog` tests (multi-line parse, malformed-line skip, empty file). `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `pnpm test` all clean (319 tests, +3 new). 7/8 phases now checked; plan frontmatter `status` stays `idea` (1 phase remains: make `killCurrent` kill every task).
- [[IDEA-65]] phase 6: gave finished tasks a persistent, machine-readable record so the history of what ran survives a dev-server restart — today it dies with the in-memory `tasks` registry. Added `TaskLogEntry` (`types/index.ts`: `id`, `taskKind`, `planId?`, `planTitle`, `agentId`, `startedAt`, `endedAt`, `outcome: 'done' | 'error'`) and appended `startedAt: string` to `agent.ts`'s internal `AgentTask` interface, stamped at all four task-creation sites (`launch()`, `startBatchReconcile()`, `startRunAllPhases()`, `runReadOnlyPrompt()` — including the always-safe `commit-suggest`/`overlap-check` tasks from phase 1, which never join the registry but still get logged since they're still things that ran). Rather than adding a bespoke completion hook at each of the several terminal-state call sites (`finishTask`, `startBatchReconcile`'s sweep-end branches, `startRunAllPhases`'s run-end branches, `runReadOnlyPrompt`'s `settle()`), centralized it in `setStatus()` itself: whenever a task transitions to `'done'` or `'error'` (the only two terminal statuses), a new `logTaskCompletion(task, outcome)` appends one JSON line to `papercamp/tasks.log` (JSONL — one record per line, distinct from `progress.md`'s prose narrative) via `appendFile`, swallowing write errors so a log failure can never take down the task whose outcome it's recording. Since every terminal transition already routes through `setStatus`, this covers every task kind without touching the individual completion call sites. Added 2 new tests in `agent.test.ts` (`describe('task log', ...)`) proving a `done` and an `error` run each append a matching entry with the right id/kind/plan/agent and `startedAt <= endedAt`. This surfaced a real test-cleanup race: a couple of existing tests deliberately leave a subprocess killed-but-not-yet-reaped when their assertions finish, and its `proc.on('close')` handler can now fire an `appendFile` after `afterAll`'s `rm(root, { recursive: true })` has already started listing the directory, occasionally failing with `ENOTEMPTY`; fixed by adding `maxRetries`/`retryDelay` to that `rm` call (verified stable across several repeated runs). Not yet exposed anywhere — reading this log into a UI is the next phase's job. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `pnpm test` all clean (316 tests, +2 new). 6/8 phases now checked; plan frontmatter `status` stays `idea` (2 phases remain).
- [[IDEA-65]] phase 5: turned the Stack panel's Agent card from a single-task view into a real stack. `agent-section.tsx` now renders up to 3 most-recent tasks (`agentStatus.slice(0, 3)` — the store's list is already newest-launched-first per phase 4's `getStatus()`), each as its own `AgentTaskCard` with its own status stamp, log accordion (own `useState` per card, keyed by `task.id`, so expanding one task's log doesn't affect another's), and stop button — so a finished run stays visible instead of vanishing the instant the next task is launched. This exposed a real gap: the stop control needs to target *which* task, but `agent.ts`'s `stop()` only ever acted on `currentTask()` (the most-recently-launched slot), same limitation phase 3 explicitly deferred. Gave `stop()` an optional `taskId` parameter (`tasks.get(taskId)` when given, falling back to `currentTask()` when omitted so the no-arg tests and any other caller keep working unchanged) and added an `isTaskDone` guard so stopping an already-finished task's id returns the same "No agent task running" error rather than resurrecting it. Threaded the id through the whole stack: `POST /api/agent/stop` now reads an optional `taskId` from the JSON body, `stopAgent(taskId?)` in `agent-api.ts` sends it, and the store's `stopAgent(taskId?)` action passes it through; `agent-section.tsx`'s stop button calls `onStop(task.id)` per card. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `pnpm test` all clean (314 tests, unchanged — the `stop()` signature change is backward-compatible and no test exercises multi-task stop yet). 5/8 phases now checked; plan frontmatter `status` stays `idea` (3 phases remain).

## 2026-07-15
- [[IDEA-65]] phase 4: gave every tick and every client read of agent state a task id, turning the single-object surface into a list. Server: `broadcast()` in `agent.ts` now takes an optional `taskId` and stamps it onto the SSE payload's `taskId` field (`pushLine`/`setStatus` pass `task.id`); `getStatus()` no longer reads `currentTask()` but maps the whole `tasks` registry into `AgentTaskState[]`, newest-launched first (`[...tasks.values()].reverse()` — the registry's Map is insertion-ordered by launch since every task gets a fresh id, so no re-insertion ever reorders it). Added `id: string` to `AgentTaskState` (`types/index.ts`) and updated the `AgentManager` interface's `getStatus` return type to match. Client: `fetchAgentStatus` (`agent-api.ts`) now returns `AgentTaskState[]`; the store's `agentStatus` field is a list defaulting to `[]`, and `loadAgentStatus`'s reconcile/batch-reconcile completion handoffs — previously reading fields straight off the single `data` object — now `.find()` the matching task by `taskKind`/`planId` in the list, which is actually more correct than before now that several write-disjoint tasks can be registered at once. Every consumer read off `agentStatus` as a single object updated to the list shape: the 7 identical `agentBusy` call sites (`plan-actions-column.tsx`, `draft-plan-button.tsx`, `create-idea-modal.tsx`, `suggest-ideas-button.tsx`, `extend-idea-button.tsx`, `actualise-all-button.tsx`, `add-idea-modal.tsx`) became `agentStatus.some(t => t.status !== 'done' && t.status !== 'error')`; `status-bar.tsx`/`stack-panel.tsx`'s "is anything active" checks became `.some(...)`/`.find(...)` over the list; `entity-detail.tsx` now finds the task actually scoped to `plan.id` (`planTask`) rather than trusting a single global slot's `planId` field, which is a real correctness improvement now that a phase run on one plan and a reconcile on another can be in flight together; `commit-section.tsx`'s fix-review commit-message prefill now searches the list for whichever task carries `suggestedCommit`. `agent-section.tsx` (the Stack panel's Agent card) deliberately keeps rendering only `agentStatus[0]` (the most-recently-launched task) for now — turning it into a real multi-task stack is phase 5's job, not this one. Updated `agent.test.ts`'s `getStatus()` call sites (`?.status`/`?.lines` etc.) through a new `currentStatus(manager)` test helper (`manager.getStatus()[0]`) mirroring the old single-slot shape, since every existing test only ever has one task in flight; `toBeNull()` → `toEqual([])` for the empty-registry case. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `pnpm test` all clean (314 tests, unchanged — a data-shape change through already-tested paths, no new branching logic to cover). 4/8 phases now checked; plan frontmatter `status` stays `idea` (4 phases remain).
- [[IDEA-65]] phase 3: fanned `agent.ts`'s single `current: AgentTask | null` slot into a keyed registry — added `id: string` (via `randomUUID()`) to `AgentTask`, a `tasks = new Map<string, AgentTask>()`, and `lastLaunchedId` tracking whichever task was registered most recently. Every task-creation site (`launch()`, `startBatchReconcile()`, `startRunAllPhases()`, `runReadOnlyPrompt`'s own untracked task) now mints an id; `registerTask(task)` replaces every bare `current = task` assignment. The substantive fix this unlocks: `admit()` previously only compared an incoming launch's write-set against `current` — the single most-recently-launched task — so once phase 2 let a second, write-disjoint task become `current`, a third launch's collision check silently skipped the *first* still-running task entirely (a live bug: e.g. reconcile IDEA-1, then reconcile IDEA-2, then a second reconcile IDEA-1 would have been wrongly admitted since only IDEA-2 was checked). `admit()` now loops `runningTasks()` (every registered task whose status isn't done/error) and rejects on any collision, not just the last one. `getStatus()`/`getReconcileQueue()`/`stop()`/`killCurrent()` keep their existing no-arg, single-task shape for now via a new `currentTask()` helper (`tasks.get(lastLaunchedId)`) — mirroring old `current` semantics on top of the registry — since turning them into a real multi-task surface is phase 4's (SSE tick/client) and phase 8's (`killCurrent` killing every task) job, not this one. Replaced `startRunAllPhases`'s internal `current !== task`/`current === task` preemption checks with an equivalent `isSuperseded(task)` (`lastLaunchedId !== task.id`) — same semantics, just keyed off the registry. Added a new test proving the fixed bug: two disjoint entity-writers (IDEA-1 then IDEA-2) running at once, then a second IDEA-1 reconcile is still correctly rejected even though IDEA-2 is now the most-recently-launched task. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `pnpm test` all clean (314 tests, +1 new). 3/8 phases now checked; plan frontmatter `status` stays `idea` (5 phases remain).
- [[IDEA-65]] phase 2: replaced `agent.ts`'s blanket `isBusy()` gate with a write-set collision check. Added `WriteSet` (`{ scope: 'suggestions' }` / `{ scope: 'entities'; ids: 'all' | string[] }` / `{ scope: 'worktree' }`), `writeSetFor(taskKind, entityId)` classifying `phase`/`run-all`/`fix-review`/`sync` as `worktree` (always collides), `suggest` as `suggestions`, `audit`/`reconcile`/`batch-reconcile`/`draft`/`extend` as `entities` (batch-reconcile as `'all'`), and `writeSetsCollide()` comparing two sets — entity writers only collide when their id sets intersect. New `admit(taskKind, entityId)` replaces every `isBusy()` call site (`launch()`, `start()`, `startSuggest()`, `startBatchReconcile()`, `startRunAllPhases()`) and is the single admission choke point now. Wiring this in exposed a latent hazard: with only one `current` slot, admitting a second, write-disjoint task while the first is still running would reassign `current` out from under it — and every completion handler (`attachReader`'s `rl.on('line')`/`proc.on('close')`/`proc.on('error')`, `finishTask`, `startBatchReconcile`'s per-entity loop) guarded on `current === task`, so the superseded task's own completion would silently no-op, leaving it running forever with no way to ever mark itself done (an orphaned process, invisible and unstoppable). Fixed by decoupling per-task completion tracking from `current` entirely — added `isTaskDone(task)` (checks `task.status`, not identity against `current`) and swapped every staleness guard in `attachReader`/`finishTask`/`startBatchReconcile`'s loop to use it instead, mirroring the self-contained-closure pattern phase 1 already used for read-only prompts. Left `startRunAllPhases`'s internal `current !== task` checks untouched — its write-set is `worktree`, which collides with everything, so nothing can ever preempt `current` while a run-all is active, and those checks stay a correct way to detect `stop()`. Accepted, documented limitation (unchanged from phase 1, resolved by the phase-3 registry and phase-8 `killCurrent` fix): `getStatus()`/`getReconcileQueue()`/`stop()`/`killCurrent()` still only read/target `current`, so a superseded-but-still-running task becomes invisible to the UI and can't be manually stopped — it still completes and updates entity files correctly, just without visible progress or a stop button, until later phases fan `current` into a real per-task registry. Added 2 new tests in `agent.test.ts` exercising the gate directly: a reconcile on one entity is now admitted while a reconcile on a different entity is running (previously blocked outright), a second reconcile on the same now-current entity is still rejected, and an exclusive `phase`/`run-all`/`suggest` launch is still rejected against any running task. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `pnpm test` all clean (313 tests, +2 new). 2/8 phases now checked; plan frontmatter `status` stays `idea` (6 phases remain).
- [[IDEA-65]] phase 1: exempted `commit-suggest`/`overlap-check` from `agent.ts`'s `isBusy()` gate. `runReadOnlyPrompt` (the shared spawn path for both `runCommitSuggest`/`runOverlapCheck`) no longer checks `isBusy()` before launching, and — critically — no longer assigns its `AgentTask` to the shared `current` slot at all, since the single-slot model can't safely represent two tasks running at once: with only the `isBusy()` guard removed but `current = task` left in, a concurrent real task (or a second read-only call) would overwrite `current` mid-flight, and the read-only call's `proc.on('close'/'error')` handlers guarded on `current === task` would then silently return without ever resolving/rejecting their promise — a permanent hang for the caller. Removed those guards along with the `current` assignment; each call now owns its `task`/`settled`/`proc` entirely through its own closure, so it settles regardless of what else is running. Net effect: a running phase/reconcile/etc no longer blocks a commit-suggest or overlap-check, and a running read-only prompt no longer blocks anything else via `isBusy()`. Trade-off (accepted, self-contained slice per the plan — no registry yet): since these tasks no longer touch `current`, `getStatus()` can't surface them while they run, so the Stack panel's Agent card temporarily won't show "suggesting commit message"/"checking overlap" progress; that returns once a later phase fans `current` into a multi-task registry. Updated the stale doc comments in `commit-suggest.ts`/`overlap-check.ts` that described the old shared-slot tracking. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `pnpm test` all clean (311 tests, unchanged — behavior change is concurrency-only, no new assertable surface without spinning up real concurrent processes). 1/8 phases now checked; plan frontmatter `status` was already `idea` (not `planned`) going into this phase, so left untouched — not all phases are done yet regardless.
- [[IDEA-62]] phase 5 (final): "Move to ideas" for a suggestion card. Split the promotion into a mechanical half (server) and a qualitative half (agent), reusing existing plumbing rather than inventing a new agent-launch mode. Mechanical half: two new routes in `server/routes/content/ideas.ts` — `POST /api/suggestions/promote` mints an id via `assignEntityId`, writes `papercamp/ideas/IDEA-N.md` (`formatEntityFile`, body = the suggestion's one-liner, `status: 'idea'`), removes the promoted line from `suggestions.md`, and calls `regenerateIndexes` — and `POST /api/suggestions/dismiss`, which just removes the line. Both share a new `removeSuggestionLine(markdown, target)` in `core/serialize/serializer.ts` that matches a suggestion's exact literal grammar line (`- YYYY-MM-DD: Title — description`) since suggestions carry no id to address by. Qualitative half: a new `buildSuggestionPromotePrompt(idea)` in `prompts.ts`, sibling to `buildIdeaExtendPrompt`, launched via the *existing* `launchIdeaExtend`/`agent.startForIdeaExtend` path (no new `TaskKind`, no new `didTaskProgress` case) once the idea already has an id — it only does the codebase-research + dated `### Log` entry, same success check as any other Extend. Client: `promoteSuggestion`/`dismissSuggestion` added to `docs-api.ts`, and matching store actions in `app-store.ts` (`promoteSuggestion` returns the new id after reloading suggestions/plans/ideas; `dismissSuggestion` just reloads suggestions). UI: `suggestions-section.tsx`'s cards are now a chromeless `<button>` (title, opens the modal) plus a trailing `×` `IconButton` (dismiss, same pattern `plan-rows.tsx` uses for backlog-idea deletion) — swapped from a `role="button"` wrapper div after biome flagged it (`useSemanticElements`) in favor of a real `<button>`. New `modals/promote-suggestion-modal.tsx` shows the description with **Move to ideas**/Cancel, calls `promoteSuggestion` then looks up the freshly-created idea from the store to fire the extend launch, and toasts (without failing the promotion) if that second launch errors. Wired into `plans-page.tsx`. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `pnpm test` all clean (308 tests, unchanged — this phase composes already-tested routes/launch plumbing rather than adding new branching logic). 5/5 phases now checked — set `status: review` in this idea's frontmatter (it had no `status:` field before this idea grew phases; a human still promotes to `done`).
- [[IDEA-62]] phase 4: added a manual "Suggest ideas" action that launches an agent to append new lines to `suggestions.md`. New `buildSuggestIdeasPrompt(ideas, existingSuggestions)` in `prompts.ts`, sibling to the draft/extend prompts, hands the agent the full idea corpus plus existing suggestions (both to avoid) and asks it to append zero or more `- YYYY-MM-DD: Title — description` lines, or make no edit if nothing's new. Wired through the existing agent-launch plumbing: a new `suggest` `TaskKind` (`types/index.ts`), `startSuggest(prompt)` in `server/agent.ts` (async — snapshots the pre-launch line count via `parseSuggestions`/`readMaybe`/`campFile` as `suggestBaseline`, same launch() path as `startForIdeaExtend`), a `didTaskProgress` case comparing post-run count against that baseline, a `POST /api/agent/launch-suggest` route (no branch-conflict guard — it only touches `suggestions.md`, not code, same reasoning as launch-draft/launch-extend), a `launchSuggestIdeas` client in `agent-api.ts`, and a store action in `app-store.ts`. New `SuggestIdeasButton` (`actions/suggest-ideas-button.tsx`) reads `ideaEntries`/`suggestions` off the store to build the prompt and sits in `plans-header.tsx`'s toolbar next to `ActualiseAllButton`. Also had to add `suggest: 'ideaExtend'` to `agents/index.ts`'s `TASK_KIND_TO_DEFAULT_KEY` map (a pre-existing exhaustiveness check on `TaskKind` failed type-check otherwise). `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `pnpm test` all clean (308 tests, unchanged — this phase only adds a new launch path over already-tested parsing/store patterns, no new assertions needed). 4/5 phases now checked — plan stays `planned` (1 phase remains: promote a suggestion to a real idea).
- [[IDEA-62]] phase 3: rendered the "Suggested from AI" section below the worklist. New `src/app/features/plans/views/suggestions-section.tsx` reads `suggestions` off the store (wired in phase 2) and renders one `Card` per entry, reusing the idea-row visual language (`size="small" texture="canvas" className="plan-row-card"`, the same `LightbulbIcon` idea rows use in `worklist-rows.tsx`) but as a plain title-only row — no `PlanIdStamp`, no status `Stamp`, since suggestions carry neither. Returns `null` when there are no suggestions, matching `ReviewQueue`'s empty-state pattern. Wired into `src/app/features/plans/plans-page.tsx`'s list branch, below `ListView` and above `DeleteIdeaModal`. Not yet clickable — the modal + "Move to ideas" flow is a later phase. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `pnpm test` all clean (308 tests, unchanged — a pure presentational component over already-loaded store state, no new logic to unit-test). 3/5 phases now checked — plan stays `planned` (2 phases remain).
- [[IDEA-62]] phase 2: exposed `papercamp/suggestions.md` over the API and wired it into the store. Added `/api/suggestions` to `src/app/server/routes/reads.ts` (returns `{ entries }` from `parseSuggestions`, same shape as `/api/decisions`/`/api/open-questions`), a `fetchSuggestions` client in `src/app/services/content/docs-api.ts`, and a `suggestions`/`suggestionsLoading`/`loadSuggestions` slice in `src/app/stores/app-store.ts` (same load-with-catch-reset pattern as `loadDecisions`/`loadOpenQuestions`). Wired `loadSuggestions()` into the existing `loadPlans`/`loadIdeas` mount-time fanout in `src/app/router.tsx`'s `RootLayout`, so suggestions load alongside the rest of the corpus on every route. - [[IDEA-62]] phase 1: added `papercamp/suggestions.md` as a new monolithic doc sibling to `decisions.md`/`open-questions.md`/`progress.md` (empty file, plus added to `scaffold.ts`'s `MONOLITHIC_FILES` so fresh `paper-camp init` projects get one too). - [[IDEA-61]] phase 5: coalesced the SSE-driven refetch in `src/app/components/stack-panel/stack-panel.tsx`. The `EventSource`'s `onmessage` handler now parses the payload and only reacts to `message: 'changed'` ticks — the initial `'Watching for changes…'` connect message no longer triggers a refetch, since the mount effect right above it already loads the initial data (that connect message was firing a redundant six-loader fetch on every page load, right on top of the mount effect's own fetches). Added a 250ms client-side debounce around the six-loader fanout (`loadProgress`/`loadPlans`/`loadStatus`/`loadConsistency`/`loadGitStatus`/`loadAgentStatus`) so back-to-back SSE ticks (e.g. an agent writing several files in quick succession, or the server's own 300ms broadcast debounce still producing more than one tick in a burst) collapse into a single refetch batch instead of stampeding all six loaders per tick; the debounce timer is cleared on unmount. Left the six-loader call itself unscoped to "what changed" — the SSE payload is deliberately generic (`activity.ts`'s comment: "the only consumer ignores the event payload... every tick as a generic changed signal") and narrowing it would need a server-side payload change naming affected entities, out of scope for a client-only phase. No behaviour change to what eventually reloads, only when/how often. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `pnpm test` all clean (304 tests, unchanged). 5/7 phases now checked — plan stays `planned` (2 phases remain).
- [[IDEA-61]] phase 4: parallelised `/api/git/status`'s three git spawns in `src/app/server/routes/git.ts` — `getStatus`, `getAheadCount`, and `getBranchHygieneStatus` are independent read-only queries (confirmed no shared mutable state between them in `git.ts`), so they now run via `Promise.all` instead of sequential `await`s; `getCurrentBranch` stays outside since it's synchronous (`spawnSync`), not part of the series. No behaviour change to the response shape. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `pnpm test` all clean (304 tests, unchanged). 4/7 phases now checked — plan stays `planned` (3 phases remain).
- [[IDEA-61]] phase 3: added an in-process cache for the `/api/plans`, `/api/ideas`, and `/api/consistency` corpus reads, invalidated by `activity.ts`'s existing debounced `fs.watch`. New module `src/app/server/corpus-cache.ts` exports a tiny `cached(key, load)`/`invalidateCorpusCache()` pair (a `Map<string, Promise<T>>`, cleared on invalidate, with a failed load evicted so it doesn't poison the cache); `activity.ts`'s watch callback now calls `invalidateCorpusCache()` on every raw fs event (not just the debounced broadcast), so a read racing a write can't serve stale entries. Wired it into `routes/reads.ts`'s three handlers (`/api/plans` and `/api/consistency` share one `work:${root}` cache entry since both call `readWorkEntries`; `/api/ideas` gets its own `notes:${root}` entry) — repeat reads between papercamp writes now skip the corpus parse entirely. Deliberately did NOT cache inside `core/readers.ts`'s `readEntities` itself: it's also called by write-adjacent flows (`agent.ts`'s phase-completion checks, `routes/content/plans.ts`'s create/update/delete, `routes/git.ts`) that read their own just-written file back within the same request/process, before the watcher's fs event fires — an earlier attempt at caching there broke `agent.test.ts`'s `startRunAllPhases` test for exactly this reason (a direct-fs-write test helper simulating phase completion, followed immediately by an in-process re-read that saw the pre-write cached entry). Scoping the cache to the two read-only routes the plan named avoids that hazard entirely. Added `corpus-cache.test.ts` (4 tests: repeat-key reuse, invalidation reload, failed-load eviction, key independence). No behaviour change to the API surface. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `pnpm test` all clean (304 tests, +4 new). 3/7 phases now checked — plan stays `planned` (4 phases remain).

- [[IDEA-58]] phase 6: untangled both `no-circular` warnings depcruise reported. `core/pr.ts ↔ core/readers.ts` was a genuine cycle — `pr.ts` imported `entityToPlan`/`readEntities` from `readers.ts` (for `syncConsistencyCommentToPr`'s plan listing) while `readers.ts` imported `resolvePrsByEntity` from `pr.ts` (for `readEntitiesAndPrs`). The `services/docs-api.ts ↔ stores/app-store.ts` cycle was the `.dependency-cruiser.cjs` comment's "already broken at runtime via a dynamic import" case: `resolveOpenQuestion` reached back into the store with `await import('@/app/stores/app-store')` to reload decisions/open-questions after a POST, which is backwards layering (a service shouldn't know about the store that calls it) and still counted as a cycle to depcruise despite being dynamic. Removed that import; `open-question-detail.tsx` (already a `useAppStore` consumer) now calls `loadDecisions()`/`loadOpenQuestions()` itself after `resolveOpenQuestion` resolves, matching how every other store-triggered service call already works. Promoted `no-circular` from `warn` to `error` in `.dependency-cruiser.cjs` now that the graph is acyclic, and dropped the stale "one known cycle" comment. Fixing the `docs-api.ts` cycle made knip's export-usage analysis sharper (it had apparently been treating the dynamic-import target as opaquely "used"): `ReconcilePreview` in `app-store.ts` turned up as newly dead (only ever referenced within its own file) — dropped its `export` keyword rather than deleting it, same convention as phase 5. Likewise dropped `export` from the relocated `PR_CACHE_TTL_MS` in `pr-lookup.ts` once it stopped being part of `core/index.ts`'s re-exported barrel surface. `npx dependency-cruiser` reports zero violations (188 modules, 725 dependencies), `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, `npx knip`, and `pnpm test` all clean (297 tests, unchanged). 6/7 phases now checked — plan stays `planned` (1 phase remains).

- [[IDEA-35]] phase 5 (final): added `syncConsistencyCommentToPr(root, ref)` in `core/pr.ts` — upserts a single sticky Scout comment on a PR with `findConsistencyIssues`' repo-wide results (dangling decision/question links, an open question blocking an already-active plan) plus, when the plan carries a recorded `audited`/`audited-hash`, whether it's gone stale since (`computePlanContentHash(entry) !== entry.auditedHash`), via a new pure `renderConsistencyComment(issues, audit?)`. Reads decisions/open-questions/plans straight off the checked-out branch — `readFile` on `decisions.md`/`open-questions.md` plus a new direct use of `readEntities`/`entityToPlan` from `core/readers.ts` (not `readEntitiesWithDerivedStatus`, to avoid a live `gh pr list` call this comment doesn't need) — same corpus `/api/consistency` reads, not scoped to just this plan since most issue kinds aren't plan-specific. Extended `GhPrViewRow`/`runGhPrView`'s `--json` fields with `url,comments` so the sticky comment can be found by its `<!-- papercamp:consistency:start -->` marker and PATCHed via the REST comment id parsed out of its `#issuecomment-N` URL suffix (`gh api repos/<owner>/<repo>/issues/comments/<id> -X PATCH -f body=@-`, new `runGhApiPatchComment`) — `gh pr comment --edit-last` isn't safe here since Scout may have posted other unrelated comments. No existing sticky comment creates one instead (`gh pr comment --body-file -`, new `runGhPrCommentCreate`); an unchanged rendered body is a no-op. Returns `'created' | 'updated' | 'unchanged' | 'unresolved'`. Exposed as `paper-camp sync-pr-consistency <ref>` (CLI) and folded into `.github/workflows/sync-pr-metadata.yml` as a fourth best-effort step. Added 4 `renderConsistencyComment` cases plus 6 `syncConsistencyCommentToPr` cases (create, unchanged no-op, PATCH-update, a real `blocked-plan-active` issue surfaced end-to-end, a stale-audit note, unresolved) to `pr.test.ts`. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `vitest run` all clean (290 tests, 11 new — no circular-import fallout from `core/pr.ts` now also importing `core/readers.ts`, which itself imports `core/pr.ts`; both only touch the cycle inside function bodies, never at module-evaluation time). 5/5 phases now checked — set `status: review` in this plan's frontmatter (a human still promotes to `done`).
- [[IDEA-35]] phase 4: added `syncPrReadinessToPr(root, ref)` in `core/pr.ts` — the one-way plan → PR readiness flip. Resolves the PR/plan via the existing `resolvePlanContext`, extending `GhPrViewRow`/`runGhPrView`'s `--json` fields with `isDraft`/`state`. When the plan's `status` frontmatter carries the `dropped` override, closes an `OPEN` PR (`gh pr close`, new `runGhPrClose`) — a no-op if it's already closed/merged. Otherwise, once every phase in `### Phases` is checked (`entry.phases.every((p) => p.done)`, the derived-`review` signal per [[IDEA-56]]) and the PR is still a draft, flips it ready (`gh pr ready`, new `runGhPrReady`); already-ready or still-incomplete plans are a no-op so a rerun doesn't call `gh` twice. Never touches plan-file status — the merge → `done` write is deliberately [[IDEA-56]]'s job, not this function's, matching the plan's "one-way plan → PR" framing. Returns `'ready' | 'closed' | 'unchanged' | 'unresolved'`. Exposed as `paper-camp sync-pr-readiness <ref>` (CLI) and folded into `.github/workflows/sync-pr-metadata.yml` as a third best-effort step alongside the existing phases/labels syncs. Added 7 new `syncPrReadinessToPr` cases to `pr.test.ts` (ready-flip, already-ready no-op, incomplete-phases no-op, dropped-closes-open-PR, dropped-already-closed no-op, unresolved). `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `vitest run` all clean (279 tests, 7 new). 4/5 phases now checked — status stays as-is (no `status:` field in this plan's frontmatter to touch, and the last phase remains).
- [[IDEA-35]] phase 3: added `derivePrLabels({ kind, tags })` in `core/pr.ts` — a pure function combining a plan's `kind` (feat/fix/…) with whichever `tags` are also recognized commit scopes, reusing a new shared `COMMIT_SCOPES` set factored out of `agent-hooks.ts`'s `resolveCommitScope` into `core/scopes.ts` (kept in sync with `.commitlintrc.json`'s `scope-enum`, same vocabulary as before, just no longer duplicated) so a free-form tag like `freshness` never leaks into a GitHub label. Layered `syncPrLabelsToPr(root, ref)` on top: resolves the PR/plan via the existing `resolvePlanContext`, diffs `derivePrLabels`'s output against the PR's current labels (`gh pr view --json ...,labels`, extending `GhPrViewRow`), creates only the labels missing from the repo (`gh label list` then `gh label create` per gap, never `--force` so a human-recolored label is untouched), and adds only the labels missing from the PR (`gh pr edit --add-label`) — additive-only, so a human-applied or previously-synced label is never removed, satisfying the phase's idempotency and non-destructive requirements. Returns `'updated' | 'unchanged' | 'unresolved'`. Exposed as `paper-camp sync-pr-labels <ref>` (CLI). Folded into the existing push-triggered workflow rather than adding a new file — renamed `.github/workflows/sync-pr-phases.yml` to `sync-pr-metadata.yml` (job/name updated to match) and added an `issues: write` permission (needed since PR labels sit on the underlying issues API) alongside a second best-effort `pnpm cli sync-pr-labels "$BRANCH"` step. Added 4 `derivePrLabels` unit tests plus 5 `syncPrLabelsToPr` cases (create+add, skip-recreate-existing-repo-label, unchanged/no-op, never-removes-human-label, unresolved) to `pr.test.ts`. `tsc --noEmit`, `npx biome check . --write`, and `vitest run` all clean (273 tests, 9 new). 3/5 phases now checked — status stays as-is (no `status:` field in this plan's frontmatter to touch).
- [[IDEA-35]] phase 2: added `renderPlanPhasesIntoBody(body, phases)` in `core/pr.ts` — a pure function rendering a plan's `### Phases` as a GitHub task-list checklist between `<!-- papercamp:phases:start/end -->` markers, replacing an existing section in place or appending one, so the `**Plan:**` line `draft-pr.yml` stamps and any other body prose survive untouched. Layered `syncPlanPhasesToPr(root, ref)` on top: `gh pr view`s the ref, resolves the plan via a new shared `resolvePlanContext` (factored out of `resolvePlanForPrRef` so the two lookups can't drift), renders the new body, and only shells out to `gh pr edit <ref> --body-file -` (stdin, to dodge argv escaping/length limits) when the rendered body actually differs from the PR's current one — an unchanged plan is a no-op, satisfying the phase's idempotency requirement. Returns `'updated' | 'unchanged' | 'unresolved'`. Exposed as `paper-camp sync-pr-phases <ref>` (CLI). Added `.github/workflows/sync-pr-phases.yml`, triggered on the same plan-branch push patterns as `draft-pr.yml`, minting a Scout token and running `pnpm cli sync-pr-phases "$BRANCH"` with `continue-on-error: true` since the very first push can race `draft-pr.yml`'s PR creation. - [[IDEA-35]] phase 1: added `resolvePlanForPrRef(root, ref)` in `core/pr.ts` — the plan↔PR resolver every later phase of this idea will call instead of re-implementing resolution. `ref` (a PR number or branch, as `gh pr view` accepts either) is looked up via a new `runGhPrView`; the plan id comes from the PR body's `**Plan:**` line or, when no PR exists yet (first push, before `draft-pr.yml` runs), directly from `ref` treated as a branch — both paths share a new exported `resolveEntityIdFromPrRef(body, branch)` factored out of `resolvePrsByEntity`'s existing `prEntityId` so the two id-resolution paths can't drift. - [[IDEA-57]] phase 4: added the "fix review comments" launch path end to end. `POST /api/agent/launch-fix-review` (`routes/agent.ts`) resolves the plan's PR via `resolvePrsByEntity`, fetches its unresolved threads via a new `fetchUnresolvedThreads(root, url)` in `core/pr.ts` (a second `gh api graphql` query alongside phase 1's count-only one, fetching each unresolved thread's first comment — path/line/author/body — refactored the shared `gh api graphql` spawn+parse into `runGhApiGraphql` so both queries reuse it), builds the prompt via phase 3's `buildFixReviewPrompt`, and hands it to a new `agent.startFixReview(plan, prompt)`. Unlike every other launch mode, this task edits arbitrary source files rather than the plan's own markdown, so `didTaskProgress` can't diff a body/phase snapshot — added a `'fix-review'` `TaskKind` whose success is judged by whether the branch's HEAD commit hash changed (snapshotted via a new local `getHeadCommit(root)` shelling out to `git rev-parse HEAD`, since the prompt instructs the agent to commit and push). `startFixReview` is async only to await that pre-launch snapshot; `launch()` itself still reserves `current` synchronously. Wired the client: `agent-api.ts`'s `launchFixReview(planId)`, `app-store.ts`'s `launchFixReview` action, and a new `FixReviewButton` (mirrors `RunAllPhasesButton`) in `PlanActionsColumn`, shown when the active plan has an open/draft PR with `unresolvedThreadCount > 0`. Added 3 `agent.test.ts` cases (commits→done, no-commit→warning, busy-rejection) and 3 `pr.test.ts` cases for `fetchUnresolvedThreads` (comment mapping incl. a general/pathless comment, bad-url guard, gh-failure fallback). `tsc`, `biome check . --write`, and `vitest run` all clean (252 tests, 6 new).
- [[IDEA-57]] phase 3: added `buildFixReviewPrompt(plan, threads)` to `prompts.ts` for the not-yet-built launch path — takes the plan and an array of `ReviewThread` (new type in `types/index.ts`: `{ path?, line?, author?, body }`, since `PrInfo.unresolvedThreadCount` from phase 1 is only a count, no per-comment detail existed anywhere in the codebase). Unlike every other builder in the file, this prompt runs on the plan's *existing* branch against an *already-open* PR, so it instructs the agent to edit whatever files each thread points at (not just the entity file), run the repo's checks, then commit and push to the current branch so the same PR picks up the fix — no other prompt in the file tells an agent to push (that's normally the app's job via `POST /api/git/push`, per `routes/git.ts`), but this launch path has no other way to land the fix on an already-open PR. Guards frontmatter and the plan's own `### Phases` list from being touched by the fix, same as the reconcile/audit prompts. Empty-threads guard: an empty `threads` array short-circuits to a "make no changes" prompt rather than rendering an empty list, since the caller (phase 4, not built yet) could plausibly launch with a stale/already-resolved thread count. Added two `prompts.test.ts` cases (thread rendering with a path+line vs. a general PR-level comment; the empty-threads guard). `tsc`, `biome check . --write`, and `vitest run` all clean (246 tests, 2 new).

- [[IDEA-57]] phase 1: extended `resolvePrsByEntity` (`src/core/pr.ts`) to carry review signal alongside PR state. `reviewDecision` (approved/changes-requested/review-required) folds straight into the existing `gh pr list` worklist pass — just an added `--json` field, mapped from GitHub's `APPROVED`/`CHANGES_REQUESTED`/`REVIEW_REQUIRED` enum, omitted when `gh` reports no decision yet. `unresolvedThreadCount` and `hasNewCommentsSincePush` need a `gh api graphql` call the list pass can't supply (thread resolution isn't a list field), so a new `fetchReviewSignal` runs one GraphQL query per PR — best-effort, only for `open`/`draft` entries (merged/closed have no review loop left), parsed from the PR's `url` so no separate remote/owner lookup is needed. There's no persisted "last agent pass" timestamp anywhere in the codebase (confirmed via research — `agent.ts` tracks progress by diffing file content, not by timestamp), so `hasNewCommentsSincePush` is instead a self-contained proxy: the latest comment/review `createdAt` compared against the PR's last commit `committedDate` — a pass ends with a push, so "activity after the last push" is the closest available signal without inventing new persisted state. Extended `PrInfo` (`src/types/index.ts`) with the three new optional fields plus a `ReviewDecision` type; `readers.ts`'s `entityToPlan` already copies `pr` through unchanged, so the new fields thread to the API/store shape automatically (surfacing them on the plan card is phase 2's job). Extended `pr.test.ts` with a dispatching fake-`gh` (`gh pr ...` vs `gh api ...`) and 6 new cases covering the decision mapping, thread/activity fetch, the "no signal for merged/closed" skip, and the failed-enrichment-call fallback. `tsc`, `biome check . --write`, and `vitest run` all clean (244 tests pass, 6 new).

Found a better existing precedent instead: `commit-suggest.ts`/`agent.ts`'s `runCommitSuggest` is a read-only, one-shot, request/response agent call (deny-by-default, stdin prompt, JSON-envelope parse) that already returns a value synchronously to its caller. New `POST /api/ideas/check-overlap` route and `services/ideas-api.ts`'s `checkIdeaOverlap` client fn (candidates sent from the client's already-loaded `planEntries`, no extra server-side file read needed). - [[IDEA-44]] phase 1: built the Tier-1 keyword similarity matcher. New pure module `src/app/features/plans/idea-similarity.ts` exports `scoreIdeaSimilarity(text, candidates, options)` over a generic `SimilarityCandidate` shape (`id`/`title`/`body`/`tags?`) — deliberately generic rather than typed to `IdeaEntry`, since the store's `ideaEntries` is actually notes-only post-unification (`/api/ideas` → `readNoteEntries`) while the real "existing ideas" corpus with tags is `plans.entries: PlanEntry[]` (every non-note entity, including undrafted ones); leaving the candidate shape generic lets the wiring phase pick the right corpus without reshaping the matcher. Scoring tokenizes (lowercase, strip punctuation, drop stopwords/short tokens) and weights title/tag/body overlap 3:2:1, normalized to a 0..1 score; `DEFAULT_SIMILARITY_THRESHOLD` (0.2) and `DEFAULT_SIMILARITY_LIMIT` (5) are exported constants. - [[IDEA-56]] phase 5: surfaced the PR badge and narrowed the status editor to just the dropped/reopen override. `core/pr.ts`'s cache now stores full `PrInfo` (number/url/draft-open-closed-merged state, via `gh pr list --head <branch> --json number,url,state,isDraft`) instead of a bare merged boolean; `resolvePrMerged` is now a thin derivation over the same cache (unchanged signature/behavior — existing tests untouched), and a new `resolvePrInfo` sits alongside it. `types/index.ts` gained `PrInfo`/`PrState` and `PlanEntry.pr?: PrInfo`. `core/readers.ts`'s `entityToPlan` takes an optional 4th `pr` param, and a new `resolvePrInfoForEntity` mirrors `resolvePrMergedForEntity`'s "could plausibly have a PR" gate; `readWorkEntries` calls both per entity (sequentially, so the second hits the first's cache entry rather than spawning a second `gh` process) and threads `pr` onto the `/api/plans` view. New `PrBadge` component (`app/features/plans/components/pr-badge.tsx`) — a GitHub-icon Stamp showing `#number state`, linking out via `target="_blank"` with a `stopPropagation` click handler so it doesn't also open the row — wired into `entity-detail.tsx`'s header row and `plan-rows.tsx`'s status cell, rendered only when `plan.pr` is set. Reworked `plan-actions-column.tsx`'s Status section: replaced the freeform 6-way `Select` (which let the UI write any of the now-derived states — a stale no-op post phase-4, since `deriveStatus` ignores the stored value for everything but `dropped`/`done`-offline-fallback) with a read-only status Stamp plus a Drop/Reopen `IntentButton`; "Reopen" calls `patch({ status: null })`, which required extending the `PATCH /api/plans` route (`app/server/routes/plans.ts`) and `updatePlan`'s client type (`services/plans-api.ts`) to accept `status: PlanStatus | null`, where `null` explicitly clears the stored override (spread-overwrites `status` to `undefined`) rather than being a no-op like an omitted field. Also dropped the "Stop" and "Needs changes" buttons from the same component — both patched `status` directly and were already inert no-ops under derived status (in-progress requires a real branch; review requires all phases checked), so keeping them meant a click that visibly did nothing. Kept "Approve & close" (review → done): harmless under the ladder, since a confirmed non-merge corrects a stale stored `done` back down, and it's exactly the offline/no-GitHub fallback IDEA-56's prose calls for. Added `core/pr.test.ts` cases for `resolvePrInfo` (merged/draft/no-PR/unresolved) and a `readers.test.ts` case asserting `pr` threads onto the `PlanEntry` end-to-end against a fake `gh`. No React component test harness exists in this repo yet, so the UI wiring itself is unverified beyond `tsc`/lint — left for a human pass. `tsc` clean, `biome` clean, 232 tests pass.
- [[IDEA-56]] phase 4: pointed index generation, worklist candidate filters, and the branch-guard at derived status instead of the demoted stored field. New `readEntitiesWithDerivedStatus` (`core/readers.ts`) mirrors `readWorkEntries`'s branch/PR resolution but over every entity (notes included, passed through unchanged) and returns the `ParseResult<EntityEntry>` shape with `status` replaced by the derived value — a shallow copy, never written to disk. Because `deriveStatus` treats an already-derived `status` as trusted input when no fresher signal is available (the "no new signal, trust what's there" fallback from phase 3), the result round-trips safely through `entityToPlan`/`deriveStatus` again elsewhere without re-deriving incorrectly. Rewired: `regenerateIndexes` and the two CLI index-writers (`add`, `migrate` in `cli/index.ts`) now source `formatEntitiesIndex` from derived entries, so `papercamp/ideas/index.md` reflects reality instead of a possibly-absent stored field; `checkBranchConflictForPlan` (`app/server/helpers.ts`, the branch-guard blocking a second in-flight plan) now reads the derived `done`/`dropped` instead of the raw stored one; the CLI `audit` command's review/done candidate filter and `agent.ts`'s batch-reconcile candidate filter both switched from `e.status !== undefined && openStatuses.has(e.status)` (which silently skipped any entity with no stored override — increasingly the common case) to reading derived status off `readEntitiesWithDerivedStatus`. Left `routes/agent.ts`'s `findPlanById` and `routes/git.ts`'s `ensureBranch` lookup as bare `entityToPlan` calls — both only consume `plan.id`/`kind`/`title`, never `status`, so there's nothing to rewire. The worklist grouping/filter/sort code itself (`plan-list-selector.ts`) needed no change: it already operates on `PlanEntry[]` sourced from `/api/plans`, which has derived status since phase 2. Added two `readers.test.ts` cases for the new function and two `agent.test.ts` cases proving the candidate-filter fix (an entity with no stored status is now picked up via its derived status; one stored `done` is still excluded). `tsc` clean, `biome` clean, 227 tests pass.
- [[IDEA-56]] phase 3: resolve and cache each entity's PR to derive `done`. New `core/pr.ts` exports `resolvePrMerged(root, branch, ttlMs?)`, which shells out to `gh pr list --head <branch> --state all --json state --limit 1` and caches the result per branch for a 5-minute TTL (`PR_CACHE_TTL_MS`) so repeated worklist reads don't re-invoke `gh`. Uses `pr list` rather than `pr view` deliberately: GitHub keeps a PR's recorded head-branch name after a squash-merge deletes it locally, so this still resolves merge state for entities whose branch is already gone. Returns `undefined` (not `false`) whenever `gh` exits non-zero or its output doesn't parse — no binary, no auth, offline, network down — so callers can tell "confirmed not merged" apart from "couldn't check." New `core/branch.ts` factors the `kind/id-slug` branch-name convention out of `git.ts`'s `ensureBranch` into a pure `branchName(id, type, title)` helper, shared so branch creation and PR resolution always target the identical name. Extended `deriveStatus` (`core/status.ts`) with an optional third `prMerged` param: `true` derives `done` outright — even overriding a stale stored value — `undefined` (unresolved) falls back to a stored `done`, and a confirmed `false` now falls through to the rest of the ladder, correcting a stale stored `done` back down to `review`/`in-progress` if the phases/branch say otherwise. 2-arg calls are unchanged, so this is backward compatible with phase 2's callers. Wired it into `readWorkEntries` (`core/readers.ts`, the `/api/plans` view only — not the shared `readEntities`, to avoid a `gh` round-trip on every reader/CLI/MCP caller): a new `resolvePrMergedForEntity` skips the `gh` lookup entirely for entities that can't plausibly have a PR (no phases yet, and neither a live branch nor a stored `done`), then resolves the rest in parallel via `Promise.all` and threads each result into `entityToPlan`'s new optional `prMerged` param. Added `core/pr.test.ts` (fake `gh` script on `PATH`, covers merged/open/no-PR/non-zero-exit/unparseable-output/TTL-caching), extended `core/status.test.ts` with the new `prMerged` ladder cases, and added two `readers.test.ts` cases exercising `readWorkEntries` end-to-end against a fake `gh`. `tsc` clean, `biome` clean, 223 tests pass.
- [[IDEA-56]] phase 2: added a pure `deriveStatus` helper (new `core/status.ts`) walking the ladder — `idea` (no phases), `planned` (phases, no branch), `in-progress` (branch exists), `review` (branch + every phase checked) — with `done`/`dropped` always passed through as stored (not derivable yet/ever) and notes always passed through unchanged. `hasBranch: boolean | undefined` — `undefined` means git is unavailable, which falls back to the stored override (or `planned` if nothing's stored). Wired it in at the view boundary, not the raw read: `readEntities` (`core/readers.ts`) now also shells out once per read to `git branch --format=%(refname:short)` (cwd resolved from `ideasDir/../..`) and returns a `branchEntityIds: Set<string> | undefined` alongside `entries`, matching branches against the `feat/idea-N-…` convention; `entityToPlan` takes an optional `hasBranch` param and derives `status` through it; `readWorkEntries` (the `/api/plans` view) passes each entity's `branchEntityIds.has(id)` through. Deliberately did **not** mutate `EntityEntry.status` itself — it stays the raw stored value, since several routes (`routes/plans.ts`'s PATCH) round-trip a full `EntityEntry` back to disk via `entityFileInput`, and writing the derived value there would immediately recreate the drift problem this idea exists to eliminate; a test asserts the raw entry stays undefined even when the derived view would say `in-progress`. Left two `.map(entityToPlan)` call sites (`agent.ts` batch-reconcile candidates, `cli/index.ts audit`) as bare fallback (`hasBranch: undefined`) since they only read `type`/`id`/`title` or filter on `e.status` directly, not the derived view — rewiring `readEntities`/branch-guards/worklist onto derived status is phase 4's job, not this one. Added `core/status.test.ts` (ladder + override/fallback cases) and two `readers.test.ts` cases against a real throwaway git repo (branch-derived statuses via `readWorkEntries`, raw-entry non-mutation via `readEntities`). `tsc` clean, `biome` clean, 211 tests pass.
- [[IDEA-56]] phase 1: made `status` optional in `entityFrontmatterSchema` (`schemas.ts`), narrowing its description to a stored override for the un-derivable states (`dropped`, closing a planless idea/`note`) plus the offline fallback — no derivation logic yet, this only stops requiring the field. Followed the optionality through the type/serialize layer so nothing else changes behavior: `EntityEntry.status` is now optional (`types/index.ts`), `formatEntityFile`'s input only writes `status` to frontmatter when present (`serializer.ts`, matching the legacy note-only idea serializer's pattern), and three call sites that assumed a defined status got narrow guards (`agent.ts`'s batch-reconcile candidate filter, `cli/index.ts`'s migrate-command `isClosed` helper). Existing entity files with `status:` set still parse and round-trip unchanged. `tsc` clean, `biome` clean, 200 tests pass.
- Removed the branch-conflict guard from `launch-draft` and `launch-extend` in `routes/agent.ts`. It was blocking drafting/extending (e.g. "Finish IDEA-56 before starting another plan" while on `feat/idea-56`), but drafting/extending only edits the idea's markdown — planning, not code work — so it's fine on any branch. The `checkBranchConflictForPlan` guard stays on the code-execution / bulk-write paths (single-phase, run-all, reconcile) where changes must land on a specific branch. This narrows [[IDEA-24]]'s "sync to main" guard to execution, not planning. `tsc` clean, `biome` clean, 200 tests pass. Server-side, so it needs a dev-server restart; interim workaround is drafting from `main`.
- Logged the decision "Status is derived from git and PR, not stored" in `decisions.md` (the settled constraint behind [[IDEA-56]]); then trimmed [[IDEA-35]] ("Mirror plans onto GitHub PRs") to match. Kept it — most of it is one-way plan → PR enrichment untouched by the decision (phase-checklist PR body, kind/tags labels, consistency-check comment, and the draft→ready / close-on-`dropped` flip). Cut the now-contrary parts: removed the "Close the loop on merge" phase (merge → write `done` + archive + commit — exactly the commit the derive-status decision eliminates; that's now [[IDEA-56]]'s derivation), reframed "Drive PR lifecycle from plan status" → "Flip PR readiness from phases and the dropped override" (reads derived signals, never writes status), dropped the `contents: write`/commit-back-to-main wiring it no longer needs, and fixed a stale `papercamp/plans/<ID>.md` path to `papercamp/ideas/`. Down to 5 phases from 6; parses clean, status stays `planned`.
- Reshaped [[IDEA-56]] from "Surface PR status in the dashboard" to "Derive status from git and PR state" after the user pointed out the original still *wrote* the stored status on merge (a commit). New framing: stop storing lifecycle status and derive it — idea (no phases) → planned (phases, no branch) → in-progress (a branch exists; branch *existence*, not "is it current", so status is the same on every clone) → review (branch + all phases checked) → done (PR merged, via a cached live `gh`/API lookup so nothing is written on merge; squash-merge means git history can't tell, only GitHub). A minimal stored `status:` survives as an override for the un-derivable states (`dropped`, closing a planless idea/`note`) and as the offline/no-GitHub fallback. Ripples through the schema (`status` → optional override), `readEntities`/`entityToPlan` (compute derived), the index (fully generated), worklist/filters/branch-guards, revises the "review is the human gate" decision, moots [[IDEA-35]]'s merge→done+archive phase, and questions whether `archive/` (a file move = commit) should exist at all. Two forks locked with the user: in-progress = branch-exists (not current-branch), and done = cached GitHub lookup (not persist-on-merge or git-history). Index title/tags synced; kept the file's current `in-progress` status.
- Closed [[IDEA-40]] ("Make sub-views real routes"): its PR #29 merged to main (2026-07-08), so promoted `review` → `done`, moved the file to `papercamp/ideas/archive/IDEA-40.md`, and set the index row to `done` — the file equivalent of the dashboard's approve-close (`archiveEntityFile` + `regenerateIndexes`), done by hand since the relaxed-guard server change isn't live until a dev-server restart. `readEntities` reads it back from `archive/` as `done` with no warnings.
- Fixed a silent approve-close failure. Root cause was two layers: `updatePlan` (`plans-api.ts`) never checked `response.ok`, so it resolved even on a 4xx/5xx and the UI treated the rejection as success (no change, no error); and the PATCH handler returns a 409 branch-conflict on `status: done`/`dropped`, so closing a reviewed plan off its own branch (e.g. after merging its PR, when you're on main or a merged branch) was silently swallowed. Made `updatePlan` throw the server's `error` message on `!response.ok`, and wrapped every caller — `plan-actions-column.tsx`'s `patch`, and `entity-detail.tsx`'s phase-toggle / add-review-phases / add-log-entry — in try/catch/finally with an "Update failed" toast (previously they'd become unhandled rejections once `updatePlan` throws). `tsc` clean, `biome` clean, 200 tests pass.
- Relaxed the branch-conflict guard so it no longer blocks closing. Removed the `checkBranchConflictForPlan` 409 on `status: done`/`dropped` in `routes/plans.ts` — approving/closing a reviewed plan isn't starting new work, and the normal flow closes it after the PR merges (when you're off the plan's branch). The guard stays on the work-starting paths (agent launches, plan creation). No tests referenced the removed guard; `tsc` clean, 200 tests pass.
- Captured [[IDEA-56]] ("Surface PR status in the dashboard", `status: idea`): a GitHub-icon PR badge (number + draft/open/merged/closed, linking out) on the entity, the dashboard server reading live PR state via `gh`/GitHub API (resolved from the branch / `**Plan:**` line, cached), and a review→done nudge/auto-advance when the PR merges. Explicitly the **GitHub → dashboard** read direction, complementing [[IDEA-35]]'s **CI/Scout → GitHub** write direction (which already plans the merge→done+archive automation but infers no state from GitHub). Prompted by the review→merge→still-in-review friction that also surfaced the approve-close bug above. Open questions left for planning: badge surface (detail vs rows), gh-CLI-vs-token auth and no-GitHub degradation, auto-advance vs nudge, and PR-state cache freshness. Added to `ideas/index.md`, bumped `nextId.idea` 56 → 57.

A queued entity that's since been deleted/renamed is dropped from the queue rather than blocking review. - Fixed the resulting "page no longer stretches full-width" regression **at the source in `~/dev/paper-ui`** rather than in paper-camp. Root cause: 0.7.0 split `Page` into an outer frame (owns `max-width: 800px`/`margin`/`height`) + an inner surface, but routed the consumer's `style` onto the surface — so paper-camp's `maxWidth: 'none'` full-bleed override could no longer reach the frame (a general regression for any full-bleed consumer, only made visible by turning the outline on). Fix applies `style` to the frame root (matching `className`/`Card` convention, restoring v0.6.1 semantics) and keeps `textureStyles` on the surface; also migrated the showcase Layout demo's texture from `style`-injection to the `texture` prop. Committed on `fix/page-style-frame-override`, opened [adooone/paper-ui#10](https://github.com/adooone/paper-ui/pull/10); shipped as paper-ui `0.7.1`. paper-camp needed no code change — its existing `style` now reaches the frame as originally intended.

- Completed phase 3 ("Build the group-aware tree selector") of "Unify the ideas and plans worklist" (`FEAT-42`). `plan-list-selector.ts` gains `selectWorklistRows(plans, ideas, filters)`, extending phase 1's `selectPlanRows` into the two-level tree: plans whose `idea:` backlink points at a plan-bearing idea nest as `IdeaGroupRow` children (via `deriveChildrenSummary` for the row-card's "2/3 plans done" text), every other plan stays a top-level `PlanRow`, and `kind: note` ideas surface as their own `NoteRow` gated by a new `noteStatuses` filter (added to `PlanListFilters`/`DEFAULT_PLAN_LIST_FILTERS`, with `NOTE_STATUS_TIER` mapping a note's `open/done/dropped` onto the existing `PlanStatus` precedence so one `STATUS_ORDER` serves both). Group/note rows sort against ordinary plan rows via `worklistSortProxy`, a plan-shaped stand-in that borrows the idea's title/id but the group's most-advanced child's status/updated/created/progress (falling back to the `idea` tier when undrafted) — so a group sorts as advanced as its furthest-along child, per the plan. An idea with no plans yet still surfaces as an empty group (Draft-plan action, later phase's UI) gated by search alone, since status/tag chips only describe `PlanStatus`; a group whose children are all filtered out (e.g. done chip off) hides like a top-level plan would. Nesting is hard-capped at one level — a group's children are never themselves grouped. `app-store.ts` gains `toggleNoteStatus`, mirroring `togglePlanStatus`/`togglePlanTag`. Added 6 new cases to `plan-list-selector.test.ts` covering nesting, orphan plans, empty groups, the all-filtered-out drop, note gating/counts, and group-vs-plan sort interleaving. Nothing wired into `list-view.tsx`/`plans-page.tsx` yet — those still call `selectPlanRows` directly, since rendering the tree is phase 4's scope. `tsc --noEmit` clean, `biome check . --write` clean, full test suite (193 tests) passes. - Completed phase 5 ("Evaluate the opportunistic adoptions") of "Adopt paper-ui 0.5.0 components" (`FEAT-35`). Assessed all four candidates and deferred every one — no code changed, only `IDEA-33`'s backlog notes updated with the reasoning. **Tabs** for `ViewToggle`: deferred — `Tabs` always renders a visible text label per item and wraps active content in a `Card`, unlike the current icon-only `IconButton` pair (label is aria-only via `Tooltip`), so adopting would be a visible regression, not a like-for-like swap. **Accordion** for `ideas-board.tsx`/`plan-detail.tsx`: deferred both — `ideas-board.tsx`'s "▾ N links" toggle needs two independent click targets in one row (title navigates via `onOpenIdea`, chevron expands), but `Accordion`'s `title` lives inside a single header `<button>`, so merging them would break the title's navigate behavior; `plan-detail.tsx` turned out to have no hand-rolled expand toggle at all — its phase-detail expand/collapse is already the `Table` component's own built-in `expandable` prop, not custom code, confirmed by grepping for `expand`/`collapse` in the file. **Menu** for `plans-sidebar.tsx`: reassessed against the plan's own stated threshold — the per-item action is still just the single "×" delete `IconButton`, hasn't grown past it, stays deferred. **Switch/Radio** for agent-config `Select`s: the only boolean/small-exclusive candidate is the agent picker in `settings-page.tsx`'s `AgentTaskRow` (`AGENT_IDS` = `['claude-code', 'opencode']`, 2 options), but it's already rendered with paper-ui's own `Select`, not hand-rolled markup — swapping to `Radio` wouldn't remove any custom code, just substitute one paper-ui component for another, which is outside this phase's "removes custom code" adoption bar. `tsc --noEmit`, `biome check . --write`, and the full test suite (173 tests) all clean (no source touched). Guard tests cover all three cases from `checkBranchConflictForPlan`: `draft_plan` rejected (with no filesystem change) while the current branch has its own unfinished plan; `update_phase` allowed to advance that same branch's own plan; `update_phase` rejected when targeting a *different* plan while the branch's own plan is unfinished. `tsc --noEmit`, `biome check . --write`, and the full test suite (173 tests) all clean.
