- Completed phase 4 ("Enforce the branch-conflict guard on plan-advancing writes") of "Paper Camp MCP server" (`FEAT-32`). `startMcpServer` (`src/mcp/server.ts`) now constructs a `GitManager` via `createGitManager(root, { watch: false })` (no SSE subscribers over stdio, so the `.git`/`src` fs watchers are skipped) and passes it into `registerWriteTools(server, root, git)`. `draft_plan` calls `checkBranchConflictForPlan(root, git)` with no target id (mirrors `POST /api/plans` and `launch-draft`'s guard, since it's always starting a plan other than any in-flight one); `update_phase` calls it with the target plan's id (`checkBranchConflictForPlan(root, git, target.id)`) so advancing the branch's own active plan is always allowed but starting/advancing a different plan while one is unfinished on the branch is rejected — both throw `Error(conflict)` before any mutation, which the MCP SDK's `registerTool` already converts into a structured `isError` tool result (confirmed by reading `@modelcontextprotocol/sdk`'s `mcp.js`), consistent with the existing validation-error throws in these handlers. Smoke-tested over stdio on this repo's own `feat/feat-32-...` branch (whose active plan is `FEAT-32`, `in-progress`): a `draft_plan` call correctly returned `isError: true` with `"Finish \`FEAT-32\` — Paper Camp MCP server — before starting another plan"` and made no filesystem changes. `tsc --noEmit`, `biome check . --write`, and the full test suite (160 tests) all clean. Plan stays `in-progress` (2 phases remain).

- Removed the FEAT-31 git post-commit auto-logger. The `.husky/post-commit` hook ran `paper-camp log-commit`, which prepended a `Commit: <subject>` bullet to the *tracked* `papercamp/progress.md` after every commit — leaving the working tree dirty on each commit, an unbreakable loop (committing the progress update itself re-triggered the hook). A post-commit hook can't write a tracked file without this churn. Deleted the hook, the `log-commit` CLI command, `src/cli/post-commit-log.ts` (+ test), the `POST_COMMIT_HOOK_SCRIPT` template, and the git-hook branch of `scaffoldClaudeCodeIntegration`; updated `about.md`, the FEAT-31 plan, and the scaffold tests. The remaining three surfaces (skill, SessionStart, opt-in PostToolUse) are unaffected; git history plus the agent's own per-phase progress entries already cover commit-level logging. `tsc`, `biome check .`, the full suite (160 tests), `knip`, and `depcruise` all clean.
- Completed phase 6 ("Document the integration and verify end-to-end"), the last phase of "Claude Code native integration" (`FEAT-31`). Added a "Claude Code native integration" section to `papercamp/about.md` covering all four scaffolded surfaces (skill, SessionStart hook, git post-commit hook, opt-in PostToolUse hook) and the `autoLogNewFiles` config flag, plus cross-references from the `scaffold.ts`/`config.json` entries in the Package Layout section. End-to-end smoke test in a fresh temp git project surfaced a real bug: `session-focus.ts`, `post-commit-log.ts`, and `post-tool-use-log.ts` each carried their own `if (import.meta.url === file://process.argv[1]) main()` self-invocation guard left over from before phase 5 wired them through `src/cli/index.ts`'s subcommands — once Vite bundles all three into the single `dist/cli/index.js`, that guard is always true, so every one of those `main()` bodies (including two `process.exit(0)` calls) fired on *every* CLI invocation, silently breaking `init` and any other command. Removed the dead `main()`/guard blocks (and the now-unmatched `#!/usr/bin/env node` shebangs and the newly-unused `gitRoot()` helper) from all three files, keeping only the exported `buildSessionFocus`/`logLastCommit`/`logNewFile` functions the CLI subcommands already wrap. Rebuilt and re-ran the full smoke test in a scratch temp project: `init` now scaffolds all four surfaces correctly, `session-focus` renders a live focus block for an in-progress plan, a real commit lands a `Commit: <subject>` bullet in `progress.md` via the post-commit hook, and `post-tool-use-log` stays a no-op for a new-file `Write` until `papercamp/config.json` sets `autoLogNewFiles: true`, after which it logs `New file: <path>`. `tsc --noEmit`, `biome check . --write`, and the full test suite (164 tests) all clean. All six phases now checked; plan status set to `review`.

In `startRunAllPhases`: (1) sets `task.phaseIndex = i` before each phase spawn so `didTaskProgress` can verify the right checkbox; (2) wraps the process wait in a `setTimeout`-based timeout that kills the subprocess and treats stalls/clarifying-question hangs as failures; (3) after a clean agent exit, checks `didTaskProgress` — fails if the checkbox did not flip (null = plan unreadable, false = checkbox untouched); (4) runs an optional `runProjectChecks` callback (lint/format/test) and fails the phase if any check is red. - Completed phase 1 ("Add startRunAllPhases loop to agent.ts") of "Run all phases with per-phase commits" (`FEAT-30`). Added `'run-all'` to the `TaskKind` union in `src/types/index.ts` and mapped it to the `'phase'` default-agent key in `src/app/server/agents/index.ts`. Added `startRunAllPhases(plan, commitPhase?)` to `createAgentManager` in `src/app/server/agent.ts`, mirroring `startBatchAudit` structure: calls `ensureBranch(plan)` up front, collects unchecked phases (`!phase.done`), spawns a fresh agent subprocess per phase using `buildAgentPrompt`, streams `[phase N/M] …` and `[commit] …` log lines, drains stderr, awaits each proc's close event, stops the loop on first failure, and calls the optional `commitPhase` callback after each verified success. Stop signal is honoured between phases. Exported `startRunAllPhases` from the `AgentManager` interface. `tsc` clean.

Added `syncToMain(mode: 'clean' | 'dirty')` function to `src/app/services/git-api.ts` that calls `POST /api/git/sync` with the mode parameter. Created `MergeIcon` component matching the style of existing icons (PushIcon, WandIcon). Added state for `syncing` and `syncError`. Handler `handleSync` checks if working tree is clean (gitStatus.length === 0) and calls the corresponding mode: clean mode syncs inline, dirty mode fires an agent task visible in the activity feed. Button is placed in the "no changed files" section, disabled when already on clean main with title tooltip "Already on clean main". Button shows "Sync to main" label with merge icon. Phase checked off, plan stays `in-progress` (1 phase remains).
- Built phase 3 of "Sync to main guard" (`FEAT-27`): added `POST /api/git/sync` endpoint to `src/app/server/api.ts` with two modes: clean (inline git commands) and dirty (agent task). Added `runGitSync()` method to git manager (`src/app/server/git.ts`) that runs `git checkout main && git fetch --prune && git merge --ff-only origin/main` sequentially. Clean mode calls `runGitSync()` directly and returns 200 on success. Dirty mode launches an agent task via `agent.startSync()` (new method) with a prompt that instructs the agent to stash/commit changes, relocate mis-filed drafts (e.g. content in legacy `papercamp/plans.md`), check out main, fast-forward, and confirm success — explicitly forbidding `reset --hard` or `clean -fd` without an explicit confirmation step. Added `'sync'` to the `TaskKind` union in types. `tsc` clean. Phase checked off, plan stays `in-progress` (2 phases remain).
- Built phase 2 of "Sync to main guard" (`FEAT-27`): extended `checkBranchConflictForPlan` in `src/app/server/api.ts` to call `git.getBranchHygieneStatus()` and block plan creation/launch with hard gate when branch is `stale-merged`. Updated the type signature to include `getBranchHygieneStatus` method. When a merged branch is detected (merged into main but remote is gone), returns error "You're on a merged branch — switch to main first" instead of allowing the operation to proceed. This block is applied before the existing active-plan conflict check, preventing any plan work on stale branches. Imported `BranchHygieneStatus` type into api.ts. The gate is hard (not overridable) to prevent silent accumulation of work on merged branches. Phase checked off, plan stays `in-progress` (3 phases remain).
- Built phase 1 of "Sync to main guard" (`FEAT-27`): added `isMergedIntoMain()` and `getBranchHygieneStatus()` helpers to `src/app/server/git.ts`. Added a new `BranchHygieneStatus` type to `src/types/index.ts` with states `clean-on-main` / `stale-merged` / `stale-no-upstream` / `dirty` / `fine`. `isMergedIntoMain()` checks if current branch is in `git branch --merged main` AND has no upstream, avoiding false positives on never-pushed branches. `getBranchHygieneStatus()` returns a typed status reflecting branch/worktree state: on main + clean → `clean-on-main`; off main + merged + no upstream → `stale-merged`; off main + no upstream + not merged → `stale-no-upstream`; working tree dirty → `dirty`; everything else → `fine`. Both functions exported from the git manager. `tsc` clean. Plan stays `planned` (4 phases remain).

Introduced a local `AuditResult` interface tracking `status` (`audited` | `skipped` | `failed`), `gapPhases`, and `skipReason` for each candidate plan. The loop now records a result per plan instead of just printing inline. After all plans are processed, the command prints a `─`-bordered "Audit summary" block: audited/skipped/failed counts, a per-plan `+N phase(s)` breakdown for any plan that received gap-phases, and a "no gap phases" note when all audited plans were already complete. Phase count is computed by reading and re-parsing the plan file after the agent process exits, diffing against the pre-audit `plan.phases.length`. `tsc` clean.

Added four helpers — `findPlanFile` (resolves `plansDir/<id>.md` then `archive/<id>.md`), `getFileMtimeDateString` (file mtime → `YYYY-MM-DD`), `stampCliAuditDate` (stamps `audited:` frontmatter field after success, same as server-side `stampAuditDate`), and `runPlanAudit` (spawns the configured agent subprocess, streams parsed output to stdout, returns exit-code success). The command now: reads `papercamp/config.json` for the default agent, iterates each `review`/`done` plan, skips any whose `audited` date is `>=` the plan file's mtime (unchanged since last audit), spawns the agent sequentially for the rest, stamps `audited` on success, and sets `process.exitCode = 1` on any failure. Imports `buildConvergenceAuditPrompt` and `resolveAgent` so the CLI uses identical prompt/adapter logic to the dashboard's `AuditPhasesButton`. `tsc` clean, 62 tests pass.

- Built phase 5 of "Build Docs page": progress timeline — clicking a progress date in the sidebar shows that date's entries in a reverse-chronological feed; when no specific date is selected, all entries are shown
- Built phase 6 of "Build Docs page": repo docs section — new `GET /api/docs` endpoint scans the repo root for README.md, CHANGELOG.md, and LICENSE; sidebar lists found files; clicking one renders its content (markdown files via `Markdown`, LICENSE as preformatted text)
- Built phase 7 of "Build Docs page": full-text search — a search bar at the top of the Docs page searches across decision titles/bodies, question titles/bodies, progress items, and repo doc filenames/content; results are grouped by source and clickable to jump to the matching entry
- Moved the Docs search input from the page content area to the nav island — it now renders as a page-specific tool after the logo (paper-ui `Input` component), only visible on the `/docs` route, wired through the store to keep the query in sync with the DocsPage
- Fixed the Focus page's per-phase copy button (`focus-phase-item.tsx`): `navigator.clipboard.writeText` was called without `await` or error handling, with `setCopied(true)` running unconditionally regardless of success — and `navigator.clipboard` is `undefined` on any non-`localhost` origin over plain http (e.g. the Tailscale/LAN access `vite.app.config.ts` is explicitly configured for), so the call threw before the feedback state was even set. Added a `document.execCommand('copy')` fallback for non-secure contexts, and a real idle/copied/failed status instead of a boolean. Also fixed the button staying hover-only (`opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100`) even while showing feedback, which hid the result the instant the mouse left the row to go paste
- Added Start/Stop buttons for plan status — on `PlanDetail` (Start sets `status: in-progress` and navigates to `/focus`; Stop sets `status: planned`) and mirrored on the Focus page next to the status `Stamp`. The `PATCH /api/plans` server handler now also auto-demotes any other currently-`in-progress` plan to `planned` when one is started, so only one plan is ever "in focus" at a time — verified against the live dev server (start A, start B, confirm A demoted, then reverted both back to `planned`)
- Caught a gap from the above: the Start/Stop button was missing from `PlanCard` — the list/board view's card, which is what's actually visible by default on the Plans page before clicking "Open." Added it there too, alongside the existing "Open" button
- Recolored the Open/Start/Stop/Mark-complete buttons (PlanCard, PlanDetail, Focus) from paper-ui's default pale cream/white fills to watercolor-style colors (blue/green/orange/violet) — since paper-ui's Button renders its fill as an SVG path behind the label rather than a CSS background, this needed a small `!important` override in `utilities.css` targeting that path directly, not a `color` prop (Button doesn't expose one). Also noticed paper-ui's own "blue" and "green" watercolor tokens are literally the same hex value (`#8FB996`) — an upstream bug, not something fixed here — so picked distinct custom hex values for all five colors instead of reusing paper-ui's tokens as-is
- Softened those button colors to light pastel washes (closer to paper-ui's own "soft blended washes" watercolor philosophy) and switched the button text back to dark ink instead of white, per feedback that the first pass was too high-contrast
- Simplified the Focus page's AI handoff copy-prompt from `Continue with phase <n> of "<plan title>": <phase text>` to `Look at papercamp/plans.md — plan "<plan title>", phase: <phase text>` — just where to look and what to implement, nothing else; the phase number was dropped and `phaseIndex` removed from `FocusPhaseItem` as part of that. Also caught up `about.md` on the Start/Stop buttons, single-focus auto-demote behavior, and the button color overrides, none of which had been documented yet
- Reconsidered: referencing the phase by number is simpler than duplicating its text, since the AI reads the actual phase text from `plans.md` anyway once it's looking there. Restored `phaseIndex` on `FocusPhaseItem`
- Changed the prompt's leading verb from "Look at" to "Build", so it reads as an instruction rather than a pointer. Final prompt: `Build phase <n> of plan "<plan title>" in papercamp/plans.md`
- Renamed "Tasks" to "Phases" project-wide, at the user's request, for clearer terminology: the `### Tasks` markdown heading, `TaskItem` type (→ `PhaseItem`), `tasks` field on `PlanEntry`/API payloads (→ `phases`), `taskProgress`/`taskPercentage` helpers (→ `phaseProgress`/`phasePercentage`), and the `FocusTaskItem` component (→ `FocusPhaseItem`, file renamed to `focus-phase-item.tsx`). Updated `about.md`'s schema docs and the existing entries in `plans.md` to match; left `progress.md`'s own historical log lines untouched since that file is append-only and never edited after the fact
- Changed the copy-prompt's leading verb once more, from "Build" to "Start" — final prompt: `Start phase <n> of plan "<plan title>" in papercamp/plans.md`
- Built "Build sidebar-driven Settings page": a left rail mirroring `PlansSidebar`'s shape with a "General" section (the existing project-info card, now the default landing view) and a "Config Files" section; descoped from the original plan to read-only during implementation — added a `GET /api/configs` endpoint that scans the repo root against a fixed allowlist (`biome.json`, `tsconfig.json`, `tailwind.config.ts`, `vite.config.ts`, `vite.app.config.ts`, `postcss.config.js`, `package.json`) and returns only the files that actually exist, plus `GET /api/configs?name=...` (allowlist-checked server-side) to fetch one file's contents, rendered via paper-ui's `<CodeBlock>`. No write/edit capability was built — `plans.md`'s phases for this plan reflect the descoped (viewer-only) scope, not the original editable-with-Save-button idea
- Built "Build the Stack — right-side status & history panel": a fixed right-docked, full-height panel (`StackPanel`) added to the root layout alongside the bottom `NavigationIsland`, chalkboard-textured with a desk-green gradient, default open and toggleable via a slide-out tab when closed. Shows the currently in-progress plan and its current (first incomplete) phase in an "Active" section, a reverse-chronological `progress.md` feed in "Activity", and a "Live" section fed by a new `GET /api/activity/stream` SSE endpoint (`src/app/server/activity.ts`) that watches the four `papercamp/*.md` files via `fs.watch`, diffs each newly-parsed snapshot against the previous one, and pushes synthesized human-readable lines (phase checked off, plan marked done, new decision/question/progress entry) to connected clients without polling. Added the nav island's horizontal offset so it stays centered in the remaining viewport space when the panel is open, and loaded Cormorant Garamond via Google Fonts in `index.html` (it was referenced by name throughout but never actually fetched, silently falling back to Georgia)

Also fixed 5 outstanding Biome formatting/import-order errors left over from the Stack panel commit

This was the plan's last phase; status moves to `review`

This was the plan's last phase; status moves to `review`
- Found and fixed a real bug while reviewing the above: Vite restarts its dev middleware in-process on every server-side file change (not just Ctrl-C), which was re-creating the `agent` singleton each time and silently orphaning any in-flight `claude` task — `vite.app.config.ts` now persists the `ApiMiddleware` instance on `globalThis` to survive those restarts. Also hardened `agent.ts` against an agent's own inaccurate self-reporting: after a clean finish it now re-reads `plans.md` and pushes a visible warning if the phase it was told to check off wasn't actually checked. Added `--permission-mode auto` to the Claude Code adapter so headless runs get the same classifier-based approval as this orchestrating session, instead of getting stuck in permission-denial loops on real file edits. Killed several genuinely orphaned `claude` processes and duplicate `pnpm dev` instances left over from the restart bug and consolidated back to one dev server on port 3333

- Built phase 1 of "Agent-drafted plans": added a third agent launch mode, `startForIdea(idea, prompt)` in `src/app/server/agent.ts`, for tasks that draft a brand-new plan from an idea — unlike `start()` (phase-scoped) and `startForPlan()` (FEAT-14's plan-scoped mode), this one has neither `planId` nor `phaseIndex` since the plan doesn't exist until the agent writes it. Refactored the shared `launch()` helper to take a plain `{ planTitle, planId?, agentOverride? }` identity instead of a `PlanEntry`, since an idea-drafting task has no plan to read those fields from. Added a new optional `ideaId` field to `AgentTask`/`AgentTaskState`; `didTaskProgress()` now checks, for an idea-scoped task, whether any plan entry in `plans.md` has `idea === task.ideaId` — i.e. whether a new plan linking that idea appeared — instead of looking at phases/log growth on an existing plan. `resume()`'s steering respawn carries `ideaId` through like it already does `phaseIndex`/`planBaseline`. No route or prompt-builder wired up yet — `startForIdea` isn't called from anywhere — that's later phases' job. `tsc`/`biome`/`vitest` all clean. Plan moved to `in-progress` (4 phases remain).

Root cause of the Luminari overuse: paper-ui's `globals.scss` defaults `body`/`button` font to Luminari, and only ~16 spots in paper-camp (page H1s, markdown headings) explicitly opt out — everything else inherited it. Added a `--paper-font-default` CSS var to the sibling `paper-ui` repo (mirroring the existing `--paper-button-font` indirection) across `globals.scss` and the 11 component stylesheets that hardcoded `$font-family-serif` (alert, list-item, select, modal, layout, textarea, checkbox, input, table, prop-table, navigation-island, button), rebuilt its `dist/`, then set `--paper-font-default: 'Cormorant Garamond', Georgia, serif` in paper-camp's `utilities.css` — flips text app-wide (table rows, sidebar nav, nav island brand bar, buttons) while page H1s/markdown headings stay Luminari via their existing inline `fontFamily.serif`. In `stack-panel.tsx`: replaced the raw `Run tests` `<button>` and the `btn-violet`/`btn-orange` Send/Stop buttons with `Button variant="chalkboard"`; wrapped Status and Commit in `Card variant="chalkboard" size="small"` to match Agent's card; removed the "Active" card (duplicated Agent) and "Live" SSE feed card, keeping the underlying `EventSource` subscription since it also drives the other sections' refreshes. `tsc`/`biome`/`vitest` clean in both repos. Created `.github/workflows/release-please.yml` — runs `googleapis/release-please-action@v4` on push to `main`, maintains a standing release PR. The `refactor` bump is implemented via `changelog-sections` inclusion; release-please's default versioning doesn't trigger independent releases for `refactor` (they ride along with the next `feat`/`fix`). To make `refactor` trigger standalone patch releases, toggle `versioning` to `always-bump-patch` or add a custom versioning plugin. 2 phases remain — Status stays `in-progress`.

- Built phase 6 (final) of "GitHub CI/CD automation" (`FEAT-22`): investigated whether `refactor` commits actually need a custom release-please plugin to trigger patch bumps. Traced release-please v17's `DefaultVersioningStrategy.determineReleaseType` (`src/versioning-strategies/default.ts`) — the method checks for `breaking` (→ major/minor), then `feat`/`feature` (→ minor/patch), and falls through to `PatchVersionUpdate` for **every other commit type** (`refactor`, `fix`, `docs`, `chore`, etc.). Since the repo's `changelog-sections` already lists `refactor` with `hidden: false`, the changelog builder includes those commits and the release PR proceeds. No plugin was needed: `"versioning": "default"` already matched phase 2's decision. This was the plan's last unchecked phase — Status set to `review` per `AGENTS.md`.

Added `scope-empty: [2, "never"]` to `.commitlintrc.json`. Test-ran `npx commitlint` against the repo's real commit style and found `subject-case` (from `@commitlint/config-conventional`) rejects the capitalized subjects this repo has always used — every existing commit would have failed the `consistency` check the first time it ran for real, a latent bug nobody had hit yet since commitlint was never wired into CI before this plan. Disabled `subject-case` (`[2, "never", []]`) to match the established style. Documented the convention in `AGENTS.md`'s new "Commit messages" section. Verified `feat(20): Settings config workspace` passes and `feat: missing scope` correctly fails. Plan stays `review`.

Wired it into the PATCH `/api/plans` handler in `src/app/server/api.ts`: when a plan's `status` is set to `done` (the "Approve & close" action), calls `git.ensureBranch(plan)` to create a branch if none exists (covers work done straight on `main`), then `git.commitAll()` with a `type(scope): description` message whose body lists every phase title as a bullet. - Built phase 14 of "GitHub CI/CD automation" (`FEAT-22`): review pass on the full plan found two bugs in the approval flow added by phases 10-12. (1) The `PATCH /api/plans` `status: 'done'` handler in `src/app/server/api.ts` called `git.ensureBranch()`/`git.commitAll()` without checking `checkBranchConflictForPlan()` first — approving a plan while a *different* plan's branch had uncommitted work would create/checkout the approved plan's branch carrying the other plan's dirty changes along, then commit them under the wrong plan's message. Added the same conflict check before `writeFile`, returning 409 with the same "finish the in-flight plan first" message used by the launch endpoints. (2) `finalEntry.id?.replace(...) ?? ''` produced an empty commit scope (`chore(): Title`) for plans with no `Id` field, which would itself fail the `scope-empty` commitlint rule from phase 8 — added a kebab-cased-title fallback scope (capped at 30 chars) for that case. `tsc`/`biome`/`vitest` all clean (35 tests, no regressions). Plan stays `review`.
- Built phase 15 (final) of "GitHub CI/CD automation" (`FEAT-22`): dropped the auto-commit-on-approval behavior added in phase 12 — after seeing it run, decided commits should stay manual via the Stack panel's existing commit form. Removed `commitAll()` from `git.ts` (now unused, including its export) and the commit-title/body/scope generation from the `PATCH /api/plans` `status: 'done'` handler in `api.ts`. Approval now only calls `git.ensureBranch()` (no-op if the branch already exists) behind the existing `checkBranchConflictForPlan()` guard from phase 14 — no git commit happens as a side effect of approving a plan anymore. `tsc`/`biome`/`vitest` all clean (35 tests). This was the plan's last unchecked phase — Status set to `review` per `AGENTS.md`.
- Built phase 16 of "GitHub CI/CD automation" (`FEAT-22`): fixed a real CI failure reported from the live GitHub pipeline — `Error [ERR_UNKNOWN_BUILTIN_MODULE]: No such built-in module: node:sqlite`, followed by `Error: warn: This version of pnpm requires at least Node.js v22.13`. Root cause: every workflow's `pnpm/action-setup@v4` step used `version: latest`, which had drifted to pnpm 11.9 (depends on Node ≥22.13's `node:sqlite` builtin), while every workflow's `actions/setup-node@v4` pins `node-version: 20` — a version mismatch that only showed up in CI since the local dev machine already has a compatible pnpm (10.12.1) installed. Fixed by adding `"packageManager": "pnpm@10.12.1"` to `package.json` as the single source of truth, and removing the `version: latest` override from all 4 `pnpm/action-setup` steps (3 in `ci.yml`, 1 in `publish.yml`) so the action picks up the pinned version automatically. `tsc`/`biome` clean; all 4 workflow YAMLs re-parsed successfully. Plan stays `review`.
- Built phase 17 (final) of "GitHub CI/CD automation" (`FEAT-22`): fixed the next CI failure — `tsc --noEmit` couldn't resolve `@dendelion/paper-ui` in any file importing it, because `package.json` declared it as `link:../paper-ui`, a relative symlink to a sibling repo that doesn't exist in CI (and wouldn't exist for any real `npm install paper-camp` either — this would have broken `publish.yml`'s output for every real user). `~/dev/paper-ui` had 30+ uncommitted files (5 new components: Accordion, Icon, ListItem, Progress, Textarea, plus supporting changes) and only a stale `patch` changeset. Committed the work, wrote an accurate `minor` changeset, ran `pnpm run version` (`0.1.1` → `0.2.0`, using `GITHUB_TOKEN=$(gh auth token)` for the changelog generator), verified `check-types`/`build`, committed the version bump, and published via `pnpm publish --access public` (confirmed with the user beforehand) — then pushed both commits to paper-ui's `main` (confirmed separately). Changed paper-camp's `package.json` to `"@dendelion/paper-ui": "^0.2.0"`, ran `pnpm install`, and verified it resolves the real registry package (not the old symlink) with the new components present in the `.d.ts`. `tsc`/`biome`/`vitest` all clean (35 tests). Documented the new workflow in `AGENTS.md`: `pnpm link ../paper-ui` for local override during active co-development, plain `pnpm install` to revert, and the changeset → version → publish sequence for future paper-ui releases. This was the plan's last unchecked phase — Status set to `review` per `AGENTS.md`.
- Built phase 18 of "GitHub CI/CD automation" (`FEAT-22`): fixed duplicated CI runs the user spotted on feature-branch PRs — `ci.yml` triggered on both `push` (to `main`/`feat/*`/`fix/*`/`refactor/*`/`chore/*`/`docs/*`, added in phase 4) and `pull_request` (to `main`). Once `draft-pr.yml` opens a PR on the first push, every later push to that branch fired both events for the same commit, producing two full sets of Quality/Tests/Consistency runs. Restricted the `push` trigger to `main` only — `pull_request` alone covers every feature-branch commit since a PR exists from the first push onward. YAML re-parses clean, `biome` clean. Root cause: `vite.app.config.ts`'s `optimizeDeps: { exclude: ['@dendelion/paper-ui'] }`, set up for the old `link:../paper-ui` symlink workflow, meant Vite never crawled into paper-ui to discover its internal `react-dom` import once paper-ui became a normal registry dependency — so `react-dom`'s CJS module was served without ESM interop. Removed the `exclude` entry, killed and restarted the dev server with a cleared `node_modules/.vite` cache. ## 2026-06-28
- Built one more phase of "GitHub CI/CD automation" (`FEAT-22`): re-checked CodeRabbit's review threads on PR #1 via the GraphQL `reviewThreads` API (most of the earlier 9 comments were unresolved threads, not still-valid findings — already fixed in code but not auto-resolved by CodeRabbit). Found two real remaining gaps: the Scout app token in `draft-pr.yml` inherited full installation permissions instead of a narrow grant — added `permission-contents: read`/`permission-pull-requests: write`. `publish.yml`'s checkout was missing `fetch-depth: 0`, the one workflow diverging from the standard bootstrap — added it. Confirmed a third thread (`app-store.ts`'s `fetchGitStatus` handling) was stale, referencing behavior already fixed earlier. `tsc`/`biome` clean.
- Built one more phase of "GitHub CI/CD automation" (`FEAT-22`): fixed a real CI failure on the release-please PR branch (`release-please--branches--main--components--paper-camp`) — Biome's JSON formatter collapses short arrays onto one line, but release-please's own JSON writer always re-serializes `package.json`'s arrays multi-line when it bumps `version`, so every release PR failed the Quality/Lint check on a file nobody had actually touched by hand. Biome 1.9.4 doesn't yet support the `json.formatter.expand` option that would reconcile the two styles (Biome 2.x feature); excluded `package.json` from Biome's formatter via `biome.json`'s `files.ignore` instead. Verified by pushing directly to the open release-please branch, which then passed.
- Built one more phase of "GitHub CI/CD automation" (`FEAT-22`): fixed `draft-pr.yml` opening a duplicate PR (PR #3) after PR #1 had already merged — `gh pr list --head "$BRANCH"` defaults to `--state open`, so once a branch's PR merged, a later push to that branch found no "existing" PR and opened a new one. Added `--state all` to the check. Verified live by re-pushing to the closed `feat/feat-22-github-ci-cd-automation` branch and confirming the workflow logged "PR #3 already exists ... skipping" instead of creating a fourth PR.
- Built phase 25 (final) of "GitHub CI/CD automation" (`FEAT-22`): fixed `publish.yml` never having run despite `v0.2.0` already being published. Root cause: `release.yml` ran `release-please-action` with the default `GITHUB_TOKEN`, and GitHub's anti-recursion guard blocks events triggered by `GITHUB_TOKEN` from starting new workflow runs — so the `release: types: [published]` event fired but was forbidden from triggering `publish.yml`. Switched `release.yml` to mint a Scout app installation token (`permission-contents: write`, `permission-pull-requests: write`) via `actions/create-github-app-token`, passed as release-please-action's `token` input — the same fix pattern already used for `draft-pr.yml`. YAML re-parses clean, `biome` clean. This was the plan's last unchecked phase — Status stays `review` per `AGENTS.md`.
- Phase 1 of "Plan storage architecture" (FEAT-24): designed the per-file YAML frontmatter schema for plans and ideas, defined the directory layout (papercamp/plans/, papercamp/ideas/, papercamp/plans/archive/), settled on id-only lowercase filename convention (feat-24.md, idea-20.md), documented the config migration path (.paper-camp/ → papercamp/), and wrote the full spec into about.md. Created frontmatter zod schemas in src/core/frontmatter-schemas.ts and generated JSON Schema from them via zod v4's built-in toJSONSchema(). Created the empty directory skeleton (papercamp/plans/, papercamp/ideas/, papercamp/plans/archive/, papercamp/assets/).
- Phase 2 of "Plan storage architecture" (FEAT-24): replaced the hand-rolled `**Field:** value` line grammar with real YAML frontmatter parsing. Installed the `yaml` npm package. Consolidated all frontmatter schemas (`planFrontmatterSchema`, `ideaFrontmatterSchema`) into `src/core/schemas.ts` as the single source of truth, with `src/core/frontmatter-schemas.ts` re-exporting them for backwards compatibility. Added `parseFrontmatter<T>()` — extracts YAML frontmatter from `---`-delimited blocks and validates against a zod schema — plus `parsePlanFile()` and `parseIdeaFile()` for parsing individual per-file entries. Added `serializeFrontmatter()`, `formatPlanFile()`, and `formatIdeaFile()` for serializing entries back to YAML frontmatter files with proper phase/log/clarifications sections. All old monolithic-format parsers (`parsePlans`, `parseDecisions`, `parseOpenQuestions`, `parseIdeas`, `parseProgress`) and serializers (`formatPlanEntry`, `formatPlans`) kept unchanged for backward compatibility until migration (phases 5/7). Added 20 frontmatter-specific tests covering parsing, serialization, round-trips, edge cases, and schema validation. `tsc`/`biome`/`vitest` all clean (55 tests).
- Phase 3 of "Plan storage architecture" (FEAT-24): built index generators — `formatPlansIndex()` and `formatIdeasIndex()` in `src/core/serializer.ts` produce markdown tables (id, title, status, tags) sorted by numeric ID. Added `regenerateIndexes()` helper in `src/app/server/api.ts` that reads the monolithic files, parses entries, derives idea statuses, and writes `papercamp/plans/index.md` and `papercamp/ideas/index.md`. Wired into every write endpoint: `DELETE /api/plans`, `POST /api/plans`, `PATCH /api/plans`, and `POST /api/ideas`. Verified the generated index output manually — both tables sort correctly and ideas show derived planned/done status. `tsc`/`biome`/`vitest` all clean (55 tests).
- Phase 4 of "Plan storage architecture" (FEAT-24): implemented archive as file move. Added `archivePlanFile(root, planId)` to `src/core/serializer.ts` — a pure `fs.rename()` from `papercamp/plans/<id>.md` to `papercamp/plans/archive/<id>.md` with no parse-and-re-serialize step. Returns false if no per-file exists for the plan (graceful no-op during the monolithic-file era). Wired into `PATCH /api/plans` in `src/app/server/api.ts`: when status changes to `done` or `dropped` and the plan has an ID, calls `archivePlanFile` after the monolithic file write. The conflict-check guard and git-branch handling are extended to cover `dropped` alongside `done`. `tsc` clean (0 errors).
- Phase 5 of "Plan storage architecture" (FEAT-24): updated CLI commands and every API route to read/write per-file entries instead of monolithic files. Added `readAllPlanFiles()`, `readAllIdeaFiles()`, `readPlansMerged()`, and `readIdeasMerged()` to `src/core/parser.ts` — async per-file directory readers that merge with monolithic fallback (deduplicating by id/title) for backward compatibility before migration. Updated `scaffold.ts` to create the per-file directory structure (`plans/index.md`, `plans/archive/`, `ideas/index.md`) on `init` instead of monolithic `plans.md`/`ideas.md`. Updated CLI `add plan` command to write `papercamp/plans/<id>.md` via `formatPlanFile()` and regenerate the index. Rewrote every handler in `src/app/server/api.ts`: `GET /api/plans` and `GET /api/ideas` use the merged readers; `POST /api/plans` and `POST /api/ideas` write per-file entries; `PATCH /api/plans` reads/writes a single plan file (with auto-demote logic for other in-progress plans) and archives on done/dropped; `DELETE /api/plans` removes the per-file entry; `/api/consistency`, `/api/agent/launch`, `/api/agent/launch-audit`, `/api/agent/launch-draft`, and `/api/agent/launch-extend` all use per-file readers with monolithic fallback. Updated `agent.ts`'s `didTaskProgress()` to read per-file directories. Updated `ideas-api.ts` and `app-store.ts` to consume `ParseResult<IdeaEntry>` from the API instead of raw monolithic `ideas.md` content. `tsc`/`biome`/`vitest` all clean (55 tests). 2 phases remain (papercamp/init migration and .paper-camp/ move).
- Phase 6 of "Plan storage architecture" (FEAT-24): moved config.json and assets from .paper-camp/ into papercamp/. Updated all code references across the entire codebase: `src/core/scaffold.ts`, `src/app/server/api.ts`, `src/app/server/agent.ts`, `src/cli/index.ts`, `src/core/serializer.ts` (doc comment), `src/app/features/plans/prompts.ts`, `src/app/features/settings/settings-page.tsx`. Also updated documentation references in `papercamp/about.md` and `papercamp/plans.md`. The `.paper-camp/` directory has been removed — config now lives at `papercamp/config.json` and assets at `papercamp/assets/`. 1 phase remains (the one-time migration script that splits monolithic files into per-file entries).
- Review pass on "Plan storage architecture" (`FEAT-24`) phases 1-5 found and fixed three real bugs. (1) `app-store.ts` imported `deriveIdeaStatuses` from `core/parser.ts`, pulling parser.ts's Node-only `readdir` import into the client bundle — broke `pnpm run build` and the dev server with `"readdir" is not exported by "__vite-browser-external"`. Extracted `deriveIdeaStatuses` into a new zero-dependency `core/idea-status.ts`. (2) `planFrontmatterSchema` had no `title` field — every plan written through `POST /api/plans` or `add plan` silently lost its human-readable name, since `parsePlanFile()` fell back to using the plan's `id` string as its title. Added `title` to the schema, `formatPlanFile()`'s input type, and all four call sites that construct it. (3) `DELETE /api/plans` didn't actually delete — it emptied the file then renamed it to `_deleted_<id>.md`, a permanent stray file `readAllPlanFiles()` would keep re-parsing. Replaced with a real `unlink()`. Updated `about.md`'s documented spec/JSON Schema and all 20 frontmatter tests to match. `tsc`/`biome`/`vitest` clean (55 tests), full `pnpm run build` succeeds end-to-end (verified both lib and app bundles, plus the live dev server).
- Built phase 7 (final) of "Plan storage architecture" (`FEAT-24`): added `paper-camp migrate` as a permanent CLI command (not a throwaway script) — anyone installing a newer paper-camp version on an existing project with the old monolithic `papercamp/` layout needs the same upgrade path, not just this repo. It splits `plans.md`/`ideas.md` into per-file entries via the existing `parsePlans`/`parseIdeas`/`formatPlanFile`/`formatIdeaFile`, is idempotent (skips any target file that already exists, safe to re-run), and routes `done`/`dropped` plans straight into `papercamp/plans/archive/` instead of the active `plans/` directory, matching the archive mechanism's end state rather than archiving them in a second pass. Ran it against this repo's own data: migrated all 30 plans (28 to archive, `FEAT-23` and this plan itself to the active directory) and all 22 ideas, zero skipped, zero warnings. Regenerated both index files and replaced `plans.md`/`ideas.md`'s content with a one-line pointer comment (kept the files rather than deleting them outright). This was the plan's last unchecked phase — Status set to `review` per `AGENTS.md`.

## 2026-07-01
- Phase 1 of "Batch plan freshness audit" (FEAT-25): added an `audited: YYYY-MM-DD` frontmatter field to the per-file plan format as the "last audited" marker. Chose frontmatter over a log line — machine-readable, no log noise, consistent with existing `created`/`updated` date fields. Added `audited` to `planFrontmatterSchema` (schemas.ts), `PlanEntry` (types/index.ts), `NewPlanFileInput` / `formatPlanFile` (serializer.ts), and `parsePlanFile` (parser.ts). Stamping is fully server-side: `createAgentManager` gains an optional `onAuditComplete(planId)` callback called whenever a `taskKind === 'audit'` task finishes with detected progress; `createApiMiddleware` supplies a `stampAuditDate` closure that reads/parses/updates/rewrites the plan file with `audited: today`. All PATCH-plan write paths updated to preserve the existing `audited` field on non-audit updates. Added 2 round-trip tests for `audited`. `tsc`/`biome`/`vitest` all clean (62 tests).
- Completed phase 4 ("Update CLI command descriptions") of "Actualize about.md for per-file storage" (`DOCS-3`). In `papercamp/about.md`'s CLI table: rewrote the `init` row to describe the actual per-file layout (`plans/` dir with `index.md` + `archive/` subdir, `ideas/` dir with `index.md`, plus `config.json` and the three monolithic files), replacing the stale `{ideas,plans,progress,decisions,open-questions}.md` list; corrected the `add plan` row from "appends to `plans.md`" to "writes a new `papercamp/plans/<ID>.md` file with YAML frontmatter." Verified against `src/core/scaffold.ts` and `src/cli/index.ts`.
- Built phase 2 of "Reconcile pass and audit gating" (`FEAT-28`): added `'reconcile'` to the `TaskKind` union in `src/types/index.ts` and a `reconcile: 'phase'` entry to `TASK_KIND_TO_DEFAULT_KEY` in `src/app/server/agents/index.ts` so agent resolution doesn't hit a missing-key gap. Wrote `buildReconcilePrompt` in `src/app/features/plans/prompts.ts`, alongside `buildConvergenceAuditPrompt`: it instructs the agent to fix only stale file-path/symbol/approach references in phase descriptions and body prose, explicitly forbidding rewriting prose that's still accurate, and enforces hard guardrails — never touch frontmatter, never check/uncheck/delete/reorder phases, never add/remove phases, never touch Log/Clarifications, no-op if nothing is stale. `tsc` clean. 4 phases remain.
